The My Company category includes multiple actions that are related to your specific company. These settings are usually managed by an administrator and are set at the company level.

, Company Info to manage details about your organizational units, including contact information, addresses, logos, and Surefire accounts.
Use separate entries for each of your company's organizational units to organize and categorize access to various marketing media. You can also organize by location.
Sample structure:
Headquarters
West Region
Branch 1
Branch 2
Company entries are hierarchical, therefore access to saved media content and permissions are inherited in a waterfall style.
For example, media saved to Surefire by users in the Headquarters unit is accessible to users that are part of a branch office. However, media content saved by users in one branch office are not accessible to users in other branch offices.

My Company
Manage Company Profile
Company Profile Account Details
On the Company Info page, tabs include Settings, Account Contacts, Company Logo, and Company Users.
Settings
In the Settings tab, you can customize your company color theme, time zone, and company phone format. Color Theme tab- Surefire will automatically set a color theme for your company based on your uploaded company logo. These colors can be edited and rearranged. Your color theme will be utilized in color branding when creating content. Date/Time tab - Set time zones and date/time display format for your company in this section. The Surefire default is Eastern. Scheduled Deployments will be set based on this selection.
Review Deployment Time Zone for additional information. Phone tab - Specify the phone number display format on outbound content for your company.
Account Contacts
In Users, Role field, you can set company users to fulfill the following roles in a Company: Primary Admin - The main administrator who makes all of the major business decisions regarding the Surefire CRM. When a Company is created, this role is mandatory and by default will be the user who created the Company. Billing Contact - The user who should receive any billing statements or inquiries. Day-to-Day Contact - The main user Surefire should reach out to on a regular basis.
These roles can be the same user or different users.
Company Logo
Review Company Logo for additional information.
Users
Click on the Users tab to view a search-able and sortable table of all the users assigned to the currently selected Company. Select the user's First or Last Name to bring up their User Profile.
Review Manage User Profiles for additional information.

My Company
Manage Company Profile
Edit Company Profile
Each Organizational Unit, referred to as a Company, in your organization has its own Company Profile entry. It includes the unit's description and contact details, as well as its Surefire account info.
You can view or manage a Company Profile page, click the Company Selection button on the Company Info page. Then select the Name of the Company whose Profile info you want to view and manage.
The unit at the top of your company's organization hierarchy is displayed by default when you click on My Company, Company Info.
The name of the currently displayed Company always appears on the Company Selection button.
You can edit Company Info details by clicking the Edit Company button at the top of the page to bring up the Edit Company Details window. Here you can edit basic fields such as phone, billing address, etc. as well as the following:
Settings
You can customize your company color theme, time zone, and company phone format.
Color Theme
- Surefire will automatically set a color theme for your company based on your uploaded company logo. These colors can be edited and rearranged. Your color theme will be utilized in color branding when creating content. Date/Time - Set time zones and date/time display format for your company in this section. The Surefire default is Eastern. Scheduled Deployments will be set based on this selection.
Review Deployment Time Zone for additional information. Phone - Specify the phone number display format on outbound content for your company.
Account Contacts
In Users, Role field, you can set company users to fulfill the following roles in a Company: Primary Admin - The main administrator who makes all of the major business decisions regarding the Surefire CRM. When a Company is created, this role is mandatory and by default will be the user who created the Company. Billing Contact - The user who should receive any billing statements or inquiries. Day-to-Day Contact - The main user Surefire should reach out to on a regular basis.
These roles can be the same user or different users.
Company Logo
Review Add or Edit Company Logo for additional information.
Users
Click on the Users tab to view a search-able and sortable table of all the users assigned to the currently selected Company. Select the user's First or Last Name to bring up their User Profile.

allows the virtual organization of hierarchically-ordered divisions (e.g. Headquarters, Branch Offices, etc.) into units called Companies. This allows you to have separate divisions and is useful for organizing and categorizing access for people and marketing media.
To access and manage a Company, use the Company list at the top of the screen and choose the Company from the list. Once you are in that Company you can view and edit the Company's Profile.
Review Manage Company Profile for additional information.

Manage Companies
Create a New Company
Go to My Company, Company Info.
Select either New Company or Create Child Company.
Select the Parent Company, the new Company will be located under this Parent Company.
In the New Company Name field, enter a name for the new company.
In the Primary Admin field, by default, the user who is creating this company is assigned.
You can change this once the Company's creation has been completed.
Select Save.
Upon initial creation, a new company is set to either Inactive or Sandbox status. The Company is not yet visible or usable in Surefire.
Select the Edit Company button to access the Edit Company Details screen. You can to complete the new Company's details, Mailing Address and Account Info and change the Primary Admin if needed.
Select Save Changes.
Select Activate Company button.
Enter CONFIRM and select Yes, I'm Sure!

My Company
Manage Companies
Company Status
Select Change Status.
The Change Status is only available for any companies created using the currently logged in user account.
Select one of following options from the list in New Status: Active - company is live and accessibly by all active Users Sandbox - default status of a newly created Company. The Company can be edited and Users added but the Company is not yet Active (i.e. not yet visible or usable in Surefire ) Suspended - temporarily suspended. This is most often set by Top of Mind administration for Companies that for whatever reason are temporarily not allowed access to Surefire. Closed - company is permanently inactive but not deleted so it maintains historical information.
Select Update

Remove a Company
Before you can remove a company you must Delete or Transfer the users associated with the company.
You cannot remove a Company if there are any Active users.
On the active Company Profile, select Remove Company button.
Enter Confirm.
Click Yes, remove this company.

Manage Companies
Create Child Company
For organizational purposes, it may be advantageous for large companies to be organized into various sub-companies known as Child Companies. Creating Child Companies is useful for structuring and categorizing access to people, resources and marketing media.
Updating company level details can only be done by Users who have Surefire Administrator roles and permissions.
Go to My Company, Company Info.
Verify you are at the top-level company, and not a child level.
Select Create Child Company.
In New Company dialog window complete the following fields:
New Company Name
Display Name Primary Admin defaults to your name
Select Save.
Alternatively, click Save & More button to re-open the New Company dialog window and create another Child Company.
A confirmation that the Child Company is created appears.
Select the Company list and verify that the Child Company is in the correct location for your organizational hierarchy.
After the Child Company is created, you can go to the Settings tab to edit the appearance of the Child Company by setting company color schemes and logos.
Review Company Color Theme for additional information.

Company Branding sets your company apart from your competition. It plays a crucial role in shaping an organization's identity and perception in the marketplace. Some of the key benefits of effective branding are:
Establishes an Identity
Builds Trust and Credibility
Attracts Customers
Increases Business Value
Combines with Supportive Marketing and Advertising
Branding is essential for creating a lasting impression and driving business success.

My Company
Company Branding
Company Logo
You can associate a Primary and Secondary Logo with a Company in Surefire. Logos provide great visuals for quick identification of Companies when working in Surefire. They can also be merged into the various branded marketing materials you want to originate from those companies. Accepted file formats for images are png, gif, jpg and jpeg.
A company's primary Logo is the main logo of the Parent Company.
If you have a regional branch with its own unique logo, upload it as the primary Logo under that Child Company.
A Secondary Logo is intended for industry logos such as EHL, EHO, FDIC, NCUA, etc. You an combine the industry logos you want to use into a single image prior to uploading them under the Secondary Logo.
Add the secondary logo merge field {{Company Image - Secondary Logo Thumbnail}} to your email Layout to include industry logos to populate on the footer of your emails.
Review Create an Email Layout for additional information.

Company Color Theme
Administrators can choose up to six (6) pre-configured company colors that are then made available for quick selection throughout Surefire for users when creating custom content such as Content Collections, Flyers, Forms, Postcards, Landing Pages, or Single Property Sites.
These colors together constitute your Company Color Theme.
Go to My Company, Company Info.
Select Settings tab.
Select Color Theme tab. Alternatively, you can replace existing colors with theme colors that provide appropriate Web Content Accessibility Guidelines (WCAG) contrast.
To adjust colors in a particular email, click on HTML and change {{ Company Theme - Color 0}} to a WCAG Surefire theme color number or a 6-digit HTML color code such as #000000 for black.
In this section you can:
Add colors to your Company Color Theme
Edit an Existing Company Color by changing the color, its label or deleting it
Change the Order in which Company Colors appear as available selections throughout Surefire Add a New Company Color
Select Add New Color.
Enter a color by: a six-digit hexadecimal color code directly into the Enter a Color* field. select the thumbnail of the color (blank if you are adding a new color) to launch the color pallet selector. Move the vertical color range slider up and down and then selecting a desired shade from the main selection area.
In the Enter a short label* field, enter a label name for this color.
A short, descriptive name that can be used to easily identify this color whenever users are making color selections is recommended.
Click Save.
Edit Existing Company Colors
Select in the applicable color.
Change the color by: a six-digit hexadecimal color code directly into the Enter a Color* field. select the thumbnail of the color ( blank if you are adding a new color) to launch the color pallet selector. Move the vertical color range slider up and down and then selecting a desired shade from the main selection area.
In the Enter a short label* field, change or enter a label name for this color.
A short, descriptive name that can be used to easily identify this color whenever users are making color selections is recommended.
Click Save.

Select in the applicable color.
Select Delete.

Status Role additional basic information
Select on the appropriate check box to perform the following actions:
Include Sub Organizations
-Displays users from the current select Company, and any Companies under it in your organizational hierarchy. Include Organizations Above Yours - If your user role (e.g., Administrator, Standard User etc.) has been granted View All Org User Profiles permission, the Include child and entire tree companies check box is available. When checked the users in org units both below and above yours are displayed in the list. Include Deactivated Users - Check this box to display any users whose accounts are in the system but are not currently activate. Export User List - Select the Export button to review user list in spreadsheet format. Disable User - Use this to turn off a user's ability to log in to Surefire without deleting their account. Profile and contact information are retained for users that are turned off . Delete User - Completely delete the user. The system prompts you with a confirmation. All profile and contact information is removed when a user is deleted. Clone User - Creates a new user with similar attribute to the current user.
Click New User button.
In the New User screen, enter:
First Name
Last Name
Email Address
User name
Select a User Role from the list. This determines the Users' view, edit and administration privileges within the Surefire system. Examples of User Roles are: Administrator - can manage everything within the entity that owns them and within all child entities Standard User - can manage their own resources and templates within an entity, but cannot manage those of superior or lateral entities and their subordinates.
Select a Seat Type from the list. This determines what permissions and capabilities a User will have within the Surefire system. Examples of Seat Type are: Surefire Admin Seat - used to manage the account.
Surefire Full Seat (aka Standard Seat) - a standard seat that is utilized by LOs.
Surefire Support Seat (aka Standard Seat) - similar to the admin seat. They are used to support an LO. Profile Seat - this seat is Non-billable.
Select the Company this user is assigned to from the list.
If you want to continue adding additional information to this User's account, select Activate user upon creation checkbox.
Select Save.
If you want to add another User, click the Save and More. The fields in the currently displayed New User screen are cleared and you can return to adding Users.

User Profiles Actions
Admins can perform several actions to or on behalf of a User from the User's Profile.
First select the user name that you want to take the action on, then edit the applicable item: Edit User - opens Edit Profile. If you are provided with permissions to edit other users' profiles, you will be allowed permissions to update users belonging to your organization or your organization's child organizations. Change Role - choose User Security and select the applicable role from the User Role tab and save. Reset Password - From User Security, select the Credential Management tab. Select Send Reset Password Email to User button to send the user a new link with a new password. Change Username - From User Security, select the Credential Management tab and modify the Username.
Select Update Username button to the right. An email notification is sent to the new Username. Delete User - To completely delete a user, select Delete a User. The system prompts you with a confirmation screen.
If you are deleting a user that any content in a folder (email collection, assets, rules, and workflows) an error message displays requesting content be removed prior to deletion. Clone - use to create a new user with a similar attribute to the current user. Disable User - use to temporarily turn off a user's ability to log in to Surefire without deleting their account.

Follow these steps to transfer users from one Surefire Company to another.

is the information that appears in the footer of your outgoing email and print media (e.g. Postcard) Deployments. It is the default signature for everyone in your organization. You can customize your Company Email Signature Block to suit your specific needs.
Your Company Bio Signature Block is the block of information that appears on your Professional Pages. You can customize your Company Bio Signature Block to suit your organization’s specific needs. This additional block can also be used as a merge field in your emails, texts, and social media collections.

My Company
Company Signature Block
Edit Company Email Signature and Bio Blocks
When you select Edit Email Signature, Edit Co-Brand Email Signature or Edit Bio Signature you are given the opportunity to customize your Company Email or Bio Signature Block contents by changing the layout or by adding / updating information and images.
Company email Signature Blocks or Bio Block are crafted and edited using Surefire 's standard HTML editor interface, which allows you to add text or merge fields, add images, and change the layout should you wish.
Review Use HTML Editor for additional information.
When you Save Changes made to your Company Email and Bio Signature blocks, you are prompted to confirm that you want to Clear Child Org email / bio signatures.

My Company
Company Signature Block
Company Postcard Signature Blocks
You can create Postcards as a Media Type for Media Content Collections. Once created, you can deploy a Postcard from the Deployment Center after which it will be printed and sent through the US Postal Service as a physical piece of printed one-page mail.
Unlike the Company Email Signature Blocks, the font styling (i.e. whether the fonts appear as bold, italic and/or all caps) of Postcard Signature Blocks are configured in the Marketing settings.
Review Create or Edit a Postcard Layout for additional information.
Edit Postcard Signature Blocks
When you click on either the Edit Postcard Signature or Edit Co-Brand Postcard Signature button, you are given the opportunity to designate what text will be included in any Company Postcard Signature Blocks but not, how the text will be formatted.
You can fill up to six lines of text per Postcard Signature Block.
Each of these six lines corresponds to a field on the Edit Postcard Signature Block screen.
Each field can be populated with either dynamic or static text or a combination of both.

My Company
Company Signature Block
Clear Child Organization Signatures
After you either click a Clear Email Signature button or save any changes made to your Company Signature Blocks, the system will prompt you as to whether you want your changes applied to any existing custom User Signature Blocks set up by users for themselves in either your organizational unit or any of its subordinate organizational units.
This process can be used for either clearing the child organization email or postcard signatures.
The three options are: Clear All User Signatures - select this option to apply your signature block edits (i.e. overwrite) the user Signatures of all users in your Surefire organizational unit (Company). This removes signatures for both Email or Postcard.
Clear All User and Sub Org Signatures - select this option to apply your signature block edits (i.e. overwrite) to the user Signatures of all users in your Surefire Organizational Unit ( Company) and to the User Signatures of all users in any Surefire Organizational Units that are subordinate to yours. This applies to both Email and Postcard. Keep Custom Signatures - select this option to not propagate any of your Signature Block edits (i.e. overwrite) to any other Signature Blocks in your or any other Organizational Unit (Company). This applies to both Email and Postcard.

My Company
Phone Number Reassignment
To ensure that no ongoing text communications with clients get dropped when the associate user is deactivated in Surefire Admins can reassign any purchased telephony/text messaging numbers from a deactivated account to an active user. The newly assigned user can follow up and respond to any incoming messages and ensure no potential client is lost.
Deactivate a User Account
When an Admin turns off or deletes a user account that contains a telephony/text message number(s), a workflow is be presented with the options to reassign phone numbers or delete phone numbers.
Reassign Phone Numbers
– Choose this option for a work flow that allows the Admin to choose an existing, active user either by typing in their name or utilizing the list option. Once a new user is selected, complete by clicking Reassign.
Delete Phone Numbers
– Choose this option for a work flow that allows the Admin to confirm the decision to permanently remove this number.
If no choice is made at this time, the numbers will move to Master settings, Telephony,
Unassigned User Numbers.
When multiple users are deactivated in bulk, no work flow displays and all associated user telephony numbers will automatically move to the Unassigned User Numbers section in the Telephony tab in Master Settings. Reassignment and/or deletion will need to be done from this area.
Unassigned User Numbers
Admins can manage any unassigned user numbers from the Telephony tab in Master Settings.
This section shows all numbers, previous user, and an expiration date for each number. Each number is available for reassignment for up to 10 days from user deactivation before expiring and automatically deleting from the system. You can select on the applicable line item to either reassign or delete the number.
Notification Center
You can get notified either daily or weekly via email of any unassigned user numbers. In the notification center and select the appropriate boxes to receive notification.

My Company
Session Length
Organizations and Users can set and adjust the time length of a Surefire session prior to timeout in 15-minute increments, up to a maximum session length of 2 hours. Admins are able to set a standard default session length for their entire Organization or, through permission, can allow Users to set their own session lengths up to a maximum session length time set by the Organization.
For Organizations, the default and maximum session lengths can be set in Master Settings, General.
The default session length applies to all company users unless permission is granted to adjust individually.
Default Session Length
– This is the standard session length for a user as dictated by the Organization. The recommended default session length is 30 minutes.
Maximum Session Length
– This is the maximum session length allowed by the company to be set by an individual.
If Adjust Session Length permission is not granted to Users, then only the default session length will apply for Users.
User Permission
Organizations can grant permission in Roles/Permissions to allow Users the ability to set their individual session length timing (not to exceed the maximum set by the Organization.)
If permission is granted, users can adjust their individual session length in My Profile, User Security.
If a user with permission fails to set their session length, then the minimum default session set by the Organization in Master Settings will apply.
A user can set their individual session length lower than the Organization default if desired.
The longest session length a user can set cannot exceed the maximum allowed by the Organization in Master Settings. Available options for timing will be limited based on the Maximum set in Master Settings.
Admins can revoke permission, and all users will automatically default to the session length set in Master Settings. If an Admin adjusts the maximum session length in Master Settings lower, then all users with permission to set their own session lengths and have set it above the maximum will automatically adjust to the new Organization's maximum session length.

My Company
Edit Duplicate Contacts
When creating or importing Contacts from various sources, there may be duplicate Contacts that you want to remove or merge. You can manage duplicate contacts using Deduplication Utility, you can set up customized fields to check for and merge duplicated Contacts in your account.
Search for Duplicate Contacts
Go to Contacts, Dedupe Utility.
By default, the Deduplication Utility screen has your Contact First and Last Name fields as the search criteria.
Users with admin permissions see a toggle that allows to search across your organization.
Click in the Search fields box to bring up a list of available contact fields to use.
Users with admin permissions may see additional choices to search the whole organization:
Select a field you want to use to check for duplicates.
Select Find Duplicates.
If the search is taking a long time to generate matches, try to limit the criteria to search for a smaller amount of contacts, if you are searching the whole organization for example, try searching only one branch.
Duplicate Contacts are listed.
This feature looks for identical matches that include any spacing in the name. Example; if you have two contacts with the last name of 'Trent III' but one contact has 'Trent III' which has 2 spaces in the last name it will not pull the contact as it isn't considered a match.
Merge Duplicate Contacts
In the Merge Contacts window, select which Contact you want to merge with from the Master Record.
Select the fields you want to merge.
Click Merge Selected Records.
The duplicate Contacts are merged into a single Contact with your merged fields added. Leaving only one contact with the information you indicated.
When you merge records: data such as past marketing events, like email history, is included in the merged record. any contact that is on multiple workflows remains on those workflows. It is advised that you go to the record and check under the activities tab that the correct workflows are there. If there are workflows that need to be removed you can remove them from the activities tab as well.

My Company
User Roles
Every user is assigned a role. This role determines what a user can access, read, write, and delete in Surefire.
The My Profile page displays your role under your name at the top of the page.
A user can not change their own role. Only another administrator can change a user's role.
By default, the system has two roles:
Standard User
Administrator
However, administrators can create custom roles and configure permissions to meet the needs of their business.

The My Account category includes multiple actions that are related to your specific account. These settings are usually managed by an individual.

You receive your username when your account is created. To find it, do one of the following: Search for emails from welcome@topofmind.com.
Reach out to your Surefire administrator.
Look it up inside of Surefire.

My Account
Username
Change Username
A company administrator assigns you a default username when they create your account. Follow the steps below if you want to change your username.
Go to My Account, My Profile.
Click User Security.
In the Manage Username tab, use the Username field to type your preferred username.
The system automatically notifies you if the revised username is available.
Click Update Username.
You receive an email that your username has been successfully updated. You can now log in with the new username with your existing password.

My Account
User Signature Block
Conditional Merge Fields - Signature Block
Conditional Merge fields offer a way to eliminate a segment or line item in an email signature block. A particular use case would be if phone numbers are labeled as Office and Mobile, and a user or co-brand partner does not have a value for one of these in his or her profile. This function allows the label in the signature block to not be displayed with an empty value.
This example is for the default co-brand signature block.
Locate the signature block.
User Signature Block
Navigate to My Account, My Profile.
Select Signature Blocks tab.
Company Signature block.
Navigate to My Company, Company Info.
Select Signature Blocks tab.
Scroll to the Signature Block you want to edit.
Select the applicable edit button.
Highlight the label and merge field of the item that you want to condition.
Example: Mobile: {{Cobrand Phone - Mobile }}
Select Conditional.
In the Conditional Based on this Field Having a Value list select the applicable merge field associated to the item in the Selection HTML field.
You can type the merge field name to access a list with related items.
In the Conditional Block Behavior field select either: (span) - if the field that needs to be conditional is in line with other items (div) - if the field that needs to be conditional is in its own cell or line
In the Add Trailing Whitespace field select: Yes, add whitespace after conditional - if you want to have space replace the conditional contents No, - use if there is no need for space
Select Save.
Once the field and its label are saved as Conditional, that area is highlighted blue. The area can be edited or removed by hovering over the field and using the pop-up options.
In this example we can see that the user has a Mobile number listed in their profile however, the co-brand partner does not. Therefore, the co-brand partners' Mobile Phone Merge Field is blank.

My Account
Acquire a Text Messaging Number
In order to engage your database with Text Marketing or use any other Surefire Telephony features, you must first acquire a Text Messaging Number for use.
Complete the following steps to locate the number:
Go to My Account, My Settings.
Click Telephony/Text Messages tab.
In theMy Text Message Numbers section, click Add New Number.
The Purchase new number screen appears.
Expand Search and select phone number list and select one of the following: Search by area code - enter your preferred 3-digit area code Contains - search for a set of consecutive numbers or letters contained anywhere in the number. e.g. 1776 brings up (631) 776-4538 and (929) 296-1776 and LOAN (760) 49L-OAN0 and (424) 353-LOAN Starts with - helps you find a number that begins with specific letters or numbers. When searching please take note that the search will start with the area code. So if you are in the 353 area code and want your number to start with LOAN you should search for 353LOAN, not just LOAN Ends with - helps you find a number that ends with specific letters or numbers. To search for number that ends in 1776 and LOAN it would only return (929) 296-1776 and (424) 353-LOAN, respectively.
Your search only returns a limited amount of numbers at a time. If you don't see a number you like, click More to refresh the search to bring up more results based on availability.
Click Search.
Click Select.
Complete the following fields on the Purchase new number screen:
Name
* - If you have multiple numbers, give each number a unique Name for better organization. Text Message Priority - If you have more than one number, this Priority ranking determines the order the system will send texts in the event that your chosen number exceeds the monthly allowance of text messages. Forward to My Cell - Select Yes, for any direct responses to a Text Message initiated from your Text Number you can choose to have them forwarded to either the Mobile Number or Private Mobile Number designated in your User Profile.
Private Mobile numbers set in this field are not visible to customers. Incoming Call Options - Select which phone option on file you want inbound calls to ring. Outbound Call Options - turn on or off the ability for outbound call usage.
Click Buy Number.
Currently there is no charge for buying a number (subject to change).
Port an Existing Number from Another Service
If you already have a text message number that you would like to utilize within Surefire, you can have that number ported into Surefire. To get the porting process started, please email Surefire support@ice.com. This process may take up to four weeks for completion.
When a number is ported from another service into Surefire, the previous service no longer has access to the number, and the number will only able to be used in Surefire.
Therefore, it is not recommended to port an existing cellular number, as this would cause the number to no longer be available on your mobile device through another carrier. It is recommended to only port numbers from an existing service you plan to discard during your transition to Surefire for text messaging.

supports personal teams for each user. A Personal Team consists of other Surefire users who fill a role or slot on the team.
For example, on your team you may have team members that you are working with such as a Marketing Coordinator, Assistant, and Processor. These roles are called Team Slots and are created by a company administrator, after these slots are created, you can assign one user to each.
Team Slots are useful when used with Workflows and Rules.
For example, every time you have a new lead assigned to you, there's a specific task such as scheduling a call, that should be assigned to your Assistant. A workflow can be employed to automatically assign the task to whichever user fills the Assistant slot on your personal team.

My Account
Personal Teams
Create Team Slot
Administrators can create a Team Slot by following the steps below:
Go to CRM Settings, Teams.
Enter a name in Team Slot Name field, such as Marketing Coordinator.
Enter a Description for this team slot.
Click Create Slot.
Once Team Slots are created, users can assign someone to that Team Slot.
You can also Edit or Delete
Team Slots. However, use caution when deleting a Team Slot as this will affect any live Workflows that utilize this Slot.

My Account
Personal Teams
Add Users to Team Slots
You can add or remove users from your personal team:
Go to My Account > My Profile.
Select Teams tab.
The team slots that are available for your organization display here.
Select the slot you want from the list.
If the Slot does not exist, you can create a new slot.
Select the user you want to assign to the slot.
Users do not have to be within your Organizational level/Branch/Child Company to be added to your team slots.
To remove a user from a Slot, hover over the Slot and click Remove

My Account
Personal Teams
Deal Teams
Deal Teams are very similar to Personal Teams. A major difference, though, is that Deal Teams consist of a temporary collection of Team Members that come together to work on one specific Deal. You could work with a different Deal Team on every Deal you work.
This is different from a Personal Team where you might have a Team Slot for your Personal Assistant that never changes (until you change your Personal Assistant).

Connect Calendar to MS Exchange
You can connect your Microsoft Exchange, Office 365 or Outlook Calendar with your Surefire Calendar allowing you to enter meetings and appointments, either manually or by using the Surefire system. Then they are automatically added to your MS Exchange Calendar.
This function does not support versions of Outlook prior to Outlook 2013, nor does the connection support Outlook access that requires VPN or two-factor authentication.
Review Microsoft Authentication Configuration for additional information.
Surefire Calendar entries are only synced with Exchange upon their creation; any changes made will not be reflected in your Exchange Calendar.

Select Integrations tab.
Click Add New Integration.
Select MS Exchange Calendar.
Enter your MS Exchange Credentials.
Complete the fields on the MS Exchange Credentials screen.
Host
If the Exchange Web Server Host URL for your Exchange Server is not automatically populated by your company, you can find this URL by going into the advanced account settings in your MS Exchange Email client.
Exchange Email Address
Some Exchange setups might require you to use DOMAIN\username instead of your Email Address. For example, if your email is tsmith@patriots.com you would format your Exchange Email Address as PATRIOTS\tsmith ( note the use of backslash "\" and not forward slash).
Exchange Password

offers the option to turn on or off notifications, as well as choose which notifications are active. Notifications are based on contact data, automated activities, and/or tasks that are assigned by the user themselves or someone else.

You can access the Notification Settings in two ways: The is visible in the menu that appears when is selected. Located at the top of the screen just to the left of your profile image.

Notification Settings Options
Turn on or Off Notifications
Auto-Archive Days - Automatically archive Notifications after a set number of days (between 1 and 365)
Subscriptions - Select which types of Notifications you want to receive (or ignore) from the existing options
Default Notification Settings
By default, Notifications are allowed, and only specific Notifications are active.
There are two options for notifications:
In App - which is represented by the bell at the top right of the user interface via email
There are also two different timing types of notifications, Real Time and either Daily or Weekly Summary. You can click to see a preview of your most recent Notifications.
To see all Notifications you can either: go to My Profile > Notifications click See All Notifications from the contextual menu that appears when you click The types of actions that trigger Notifications include, but are not limited to:
Assign Contact
Contact Birthday
Deployment Start
Form Submission
Zapier Submission
Incoming Text Messages
Suggested Deployment
Incoming Text Messages notification links expire after 5 days.
Notification Center
In the Notification Center you can see a full summary of your Notifications and have the option to perform the following actions:
Archive - Remove notifications from your current in box and move them to the Archived tab where they can be referenced later if necessary.
Filter - You can choose to filter by Notification Types
Search - Type a word or phrase to search notifications in your Current or Archived tabs. A search only affects the active tab.

My Account
Notification Center
Opportunity Alerts - Rate Alerts
A Rate Alert is a special and specific type of notification in Surefire which tells the user when a past client's current rate is higher than the current market conditions, mortgage rates today.
Rate Alert Requirements
Please note that our Rate Alert notifications are generated only for Conventional, FHA, VA, and USDA loan types with Fixed Amortization for 15 or 30-year terms.
Rate Alert notifications require:
First Lien
Amortization Type
Loan Rate
Loan Type
Term (months)
Primary Deal
Closing Date fields to be populated using the closed deal policy
If you have any questions regarding these requirements, please follow up with your company's Surefire administrator or a Surefire representative to assist you with configuring your Rate Alert notifications. Any contacts who meet the set criteria for a Rate Alert will come to you via email and/or in-app notification each day at 9 AM in your timezone.
An automation based off a Rate Alert - Rate Alert Received is available within Surefire 's powerful rule engine to trigger automation that you desire. An example of this is to tag the contact with "Rate Alert Notice", send the contact owner an immediate text message, as well as a reminder to follow-up with the rate alert opportunity 2 days after the initial rate alert is received. Please note, the mortgage product must be selected within the rule for the rate alert rule trigger to be available.
The Admin configures how much difference in the rate will trigger a Rate Alert. For example, a contact with a home loan that has a 5.000% rate may not benefit from refinancing to a rate of 4.750%, even though 4.750% is lower than 5%.
This number is adjustable so the Admin can select how much difference between the client's current rate, and the market rate (the mortgage rates today) would be a large enough gap to ‘make it worth it’ for their client.
The Admin configures the desired difference in the rate (the Rate Threshold) so that the notification occurs when the desired difference in rate is met, for example, -0.500% or greater.
Set Up Rate Alerts - Admin

Click Save.
If the Opportunity Alerts - It's Listed is on, and a property, based on physical address associated with a contact in your database goes on sale, the owner of that contact gets an alert Email or In-App Notification. If there is no physical address for a contact record, the system will look at the contact record's mailing address.

Impersonation is an Administrator option that gives you the ability to log into the account of any user in your organization. When using Impersonation, you are essentially logging in as that user and seeing everything that they see in their account.
This can be used for troubleshooting an issue and other administrative use cases.
To Impersonate a user:
In your profile list, select the Impersonate.
Select the user from the list.
A Red Bar appears at the top of the screen indicating that you are impersonating a user. You are now using Surefire as this User.
When impersonating a user you can view the user's activity by navigating to My Account, My Profile.
In the user's profile you can view: delegation of impersonation, successful impersonations, user log ins, and user data updates.
Click the X in the red bar to exit impersonation mode.
You return back to your own account.

My Account
Impersonate a User
Grant Impersonation Access
Impersonation Access is turned on by default. This setting allows your company administrator or Surefire Support to access to your account for troubleshooting and other administrative purposes.
If you have chosen to turn off impersonation access you can change it and grant access to your admin for either a limited time or lifetime. You will receive your admin request via email.
Review Turn off Impersonation Access, for additional information.
To grant Impersonation Access:
Go to My Account, My Settings.
Select Access to My Account tab.
In Pending Impersonations click Approve.
You will be prompted to approve this Impersonation Request.

Impersonate a User

All user Impersonation Access is turned on by default allowing the admin to Impersonate a user's account.
If a user chooses to turn off this option, an admin must send them an Impersonation Access Request to gain access to the users account.
To turn off Impersonation:
Go to My Account, My Settings.
Select Access to My Account tab.
In Current Impersonation Access, click the All admins can login as me toggle..

My Account
Add a Delegate
You can Add a Delegate to your Account to grant specific permissions to another User or Team Member in your organization. This is a useful function if you have someone in an assistant role that you wish to have access to your account to perform tasks on your behalf.
Your Delegate can update your Contact list, add new Contacts, or send a Deployment on your behalf depending on the permissions you grant them.
You can add either a User or a Team Member as a Delegate. Whether assigning a User directly or indirectly via a Team Member Role, they will function exactly the same as a Delegate.
The main difference is that by using a Team Member as a Delegate, the User in your Delegate role automatically changes if you ever change the User you have in the Team Member slot.
For example, you have a Loan Officer Assistant Team Member slot that is filled by Steve. You want your assistant to be able to act as a Delegate and send emails, add contacts, etc. on your behalf so assign your Loan Officer Assistant as a Delegate (i.e. you do not directly assign the User Steve as a Delegate.)
If you get a new assistant and assign them to your Loan Officer Assistant slot, they will automatically have the same Delegate rights to your account.
To add a user delegation:
Go to My Account, My Settings.
Select Access to My Account tab.
Click Add New Delegation.
Select the user or Team Slot from the list of names.
Select the applicable delegation permissions. Create - add a new Contact to your account. Read - view your Contacts list. Update - update or edit any information in your Contact's Record. This includes adding notes, tasks and sending invites to your Contacts on your behalf. Delete - remove any of your Contacts. Deploy - send a Deployment on your behalf. Billable - execute any functions that will result in User being billed.
Click Save Delegation.

My Account
Add a Delegate
Delegation Permissions
Delegation gives you the ability to assign specific permissions to a user on your account. Granting delegate permissions gives your delegate access to your contacts and allows them to take actions with those contacts on your behalf.
Once a Delegate's Permissions are granted, they cannot be edited. If you need to edit them, you must remove the delegate and re-add them with the new permissions.
The permissions types that can be assigned to aDelegate are: Create - add a new Contact to your account. Read - view your Contacts list. Update - update or edit any information in your Contact's Record. This includes adding notes, tasks and sending invites to your Contacts on your behalf. Delete - remove any of your Contacts. Deploy - send a Deployment on your behalf. Billable - execute any functions that will result in User being billed.

My Account
Add a Delegate
Send a Deployment as a Delegate
As a delegate, you may need to Send Deployments on behalf of another user in your organization. Creating a deployment as a delegate is essentially the same as sending a normal Deployment. The key differences are in the Who is This Deployment For? option and the Audience Builder.
Review Create a Deployment for additional information.
Send via Deployment Center
To send a deployment using the Create a Deployment process, use the following :
Under the General section,
Under Who is the deployment for?
Select the user on whose behalf you will be sending the deployment.
When you get to the Audience Builder section, your available Contacts will now be your Delegate's Contacts instead of your own.
The recipients will receive an email from your Delegate. To the recipient, it will appear no different than if the delegate had sent the email.
Sending from the Contact Record
All deployments sent via a delegate are sent through the Deployment Center.

Once the Delegation is removed, the User no longer has any permissions on your account.

Email Delivery Set Up
Request email server set up is required to authorize Surefire to send emails on your behalf. Access the Resource Center and complete the following steps to submit a case:
In the Product List select Surefire In Request type, select CRM Settings
Select Next.
Select Request Form for Email Optimization Setup.
Complete the form.

Surefire CRM is a third-party email delivery service. To effectively use our service, you must edit the DNS server of your email domain to authorize Surefire to send emails on your behalf. Your IT Department or IT Consultant will usually make these edits. If you do not have an IT department, we will assist you. If you do not make these changes, you may not receive the emails we send to you, and the emails you send to your contacts may go to Spam folders. It is important that you make these changes as soon as possible to ensure trouble-free email delivery.

Organize/Submit Data for Users Self-Guided Accounts Admin Actions Surefire performs a one-time upload of your contact data. Submit all spreadsheets in a single ticket. Follow the upload requirements and data formatting best practices.
Review Data File Management for additional information
Data Upload Requirements
Export or create a spreadsheet with relevant data fields
Save in Excel .xlsx or .csv format
List column headers to identify the content for every column
Each contact must have a first and last name to be uploaded
List a contact type for each contact
If there is a name on the spreadsheet, a contact type must be assigned for upload
Contact types must exactly match those in Surefire Review Create a Contact Type for additional information.
List the User/Loan Officer that should own the contacts in Surefire for each contact Surefire uses email, birthday, or mobile number to match duplicate contacts – at least one of these fields should be listed for each contact.
For It's Listed and Rate Alerts to trigger, you’ll also need to include the following:
Rate Alerts: Primary Deal Closing Date, Occupancy Date, and Lien position
It's Listed Alerts: Mailing or Physical address on file
Items that do not upload to Surefire Extensions or notes listed after the 10-digit phone number
Fake phone numbers. Examples: (555) 555-5555 or (999) 999-9999
General terms that fill in blank fields. Examples: N/A, null, unknown and TBD
Copyright symbols ®
Irregular characters. Examples: [ ] < > ï ã€€ â™ ® ï¿½ Ê
Common Issues with Spreadsheets
User does not have an account in Surefire Contact type does not exist in Surefire Missing First or Last Name
General terms that fill blank fields
Fake numbers
Missing contact type - a contact type must be listed for each name on the spreadsheet
Data Submission
Submit a case in the Resource Center. This sends the information to the Surefire data team for upload.
Log into Surefire.
Select the drop down in the upper right-hand corner next to your name.
Select Resource Center a separate browser window opens.
Select Contact Support.
Select Next.
Select Surefire product.
In Request Type select My Account.
In the Subject line enter Historical Data – Your Company Name.
In the Description, identify that you are on-boarding and submitting your data for upload.
Choose file(s) for upload, be sure to include all spreadsheets in a single ticket.
In Severity, select General Help & Configuration.
Select Next.
Review the summary of the case.
Validate or update if needed.
Select Submit a New Case.
We can only respond to inquiries from Surefire seat holders
After the information is submitted, the data team reviews and follows up with any questions or issues related to the upload. A confirmation email is sent when complete.
Attachment limit is 25MB. All file types are accepted. Additional attachments can be added once the case has been submitted.

Marketing Automation for Self-Guided Accounts - Power Messaging
Power Messaging requires Twilio registration and is the texting feature in Surefire. There is a pay per use fee. If you have questions about pricing, check with your sales rep. Surefire uses Twilio as their phone servicing provider. To prevent blocking, Twilio requires all phones numbers for texting to be fully registered.
Register your company by filling out the Twilio Registration for Power Messaging form.
A profile is created in Twilio and submitted for approval.
During this process, you’ll still be able to use Power Messaging.
Continued use of texting will be contingent on Twilio’s final approval of your profile.
Complete Acquire a Text Messaging Number to secure a phone number for texting.
Create a Surefire ticket to have the number assigned to your Twilio profile:
Access the ticketing system through the Help Center, drop down in the upper right-hand corner next to your name. in the Subject enter Register Text Number in the Body include the user’s name and acquired number for texting
We only respond to inquiries from Surefire seat holders.

Integrations
Encompass® Surefire Direct Integration
Direct integration that turns on one-way synchronization of loan data from Encompass® to Surefire is designed to streamline the capture of essential mortgage fields, borrower details, and affiliated deal team member information, ensuring Surefire remains up to date with the latest loan activity.
The integration relies on visibility into the Encompass®
LOS pipeline and is triggered by updates made to the loan last modified field in Encompass®. Once the integration is active and configured, loans that meet the relevant criteria are automatically imported into Surefire through a scheduled batch process.
Field Mapping
By default, the integration is setup to capture the following data in Surefire:
Primary and Co-Borrower Information
Loan-Specific Data (full list of mapped fields linked below)
Milestones (mapped directly from Encompass pipeline)
Affiliated Contacts (e.g., buying agents, listing agents, processors)
A comprehensive list of mapped fields can be found
Encompass® Surefire Data Map.
Client Setup Requirements in the LOS
To ensure seamless integration, clients must complete any customization in their Encompass®
LOS, including:
Define Custom Fields – Create necessary custom data points or fields available for mapping.
Configure Folders & Filters – Structure loan pipeline with appropriate folders and filters to ensure only relevant loans are included in the sync.
Changes made to the Encompass loan file are shared with Surefire to ensure the most current information is available.
Review Custom Fields / Loan Folder Setup for additional information on configuring Encompass.
Professional Services and Additional Assistance
Encompass®
Direct Integration with Surefire requires assistance from the IMT professional services team. Contact the professional services team or your sales representative to discuss scope, pricing and availability.
For advanced configuration needs, complex business logic, or additional customization, professional services may be required. These services are not included in the standard integration and require additional fees.

Integrations
Encompass® Consumer Connect (ECC) Pre-Population
Encompass®
Consumer Connect (ECC) Pre-Population Surefire 's pre-population to ECC’s feature is designed to streamline the mortgage application process by automatically filling in borrower information across systems.
A Loan Officer or team member can send an ECC invite via Surefire email or text, allowing the borrower to engage with the campaign and auto-fill their loan application for a seamless experience. Borrower Receives Campaign Email - Borrower reviews email and clicks the link to start a loan application. Borrower Initiates Application - Borrower accesses a lender’s customized ECC Portal and sees their information pre-populated. Borrower confirms the information and continues the loan application.
The Loan Officer can access, the pre-populated application in Encompass®, review it, and proceed with pricing and processing quickly, often within minutes.
See Create an Email for Content Collection and Insert ECC Invite to Apply for additional information.

does integrate with it. Procedures for integration are included.

Integrations
Integrate with CardTapp
If your company has a CardTapp account, it can be integrated with Surefire if you have an available Webhook slot in your Surefire account. If you are interested pursuing this integration email Surefire support@ice.com.
This integration can automatically or selectively deliver the CardTapp mobile app download URL in a Text message. This encourages the user's contacts to begin or remain engaged in the mortgage process with a valuable resource.
Based on conditions established in Surefire, a Webhook can be created to deliver CardTapp a contact's information. Custom Rules can determine if the Webhook should deliver data automatically to CardTapp, or manual selection to deliver data can be used on a per contact basis.
CardTapp can then return an update to that contact, which will add a unique CardTapp moblie app URL to that contact's profile in a custom field. The value of that custom field can then be delivered to the contact to request them to install the CardTapp app. The delivery of this app URL can also be automated through Custom Rules. In addition, Surefire can also track how many times a contact has shared the user's CardTapp mobile app with others.

Integrations
Integration Floify
In order to initiate an integration with Floify, three keys are required. An APIKey and a ClientKey from Surefire, and a Floify API Key obtained from Floify.Only admins can retrieve this key.
APIKey
A representative at Top of Mind must create an APIKey.
Go to My Company, Company Info.
Select API in the horizontal menu on that page
Locate the Data Integration Policy Key.
If an APIKey is not present, contact Surefire support@ice.com.
Some admins may see a Public API Policy Key; that is not needed for the Floify integration.
ClientKey
A ClientKey is located by going to any user profile. Select Integrations, the ClientKey is the Zapier Key
If an integration is set at a company level, then an admin's ClientKey must be used for routing data to various users. A lower tiered user's ClientKey would not be able to load data to another user that is not below that user in the role/company hierarchy.
It is suggested that a user profile for Floify be created for Enterprise accounts, most likely admin level for ClientKey use. The name of that user profile is what is important as when Floify delivers data to add/update a contact, both the upload job and the contact history will then denote that the Floify was responsible for the add/update.
Floify UI Input
After the Surefire Keys are obtained, the keys are enter into the Floify UI.
Go to Company Settings.
Access Company Settings. You may need to change your Team.
In Change Team, click on Company Dashboard link.
Select Integrations tab.
Scroll to the CRM Integrations area, select edit on the Surefire entry.
Enter the Surefire keys in apikey and clientkey fields. Enter the Floify key in floifyapikey.
This key is obtained from Floify.
Select Save.
After the keys are installed, Floify begins sending data to Surefire. A Top of Mind representative will have already cloned down the basic map for Floify data receipt. The basic map will gather contact level data only. If you are LOS integrated with Surefire, then it is not suggested to incorporate loan level information as your LOS will populate that information to Surefire.
Floify Company Dashboard - Surefire Sync Email Address
Check your Surefire Sync email in Floify by going into the Company Dashboard. Click Edit team CRM integration properties and verify that the email you use for Surefire is in the popup box.
This will ensure that when Floify syncs with Surefire syncs to the correct user. This must be done for the sync to work properly
Loan / Milestone Mapping
If you are not LOS integrated with Surefire, then we have an answer for automatic deployment of in process emails. Floify Milestones can be mapped to Surefire Sales phases, along with basic loan information. To get started, it's best to have browser windows opened for both Surefire and Floify.
In Surefire:
Navigate to Sales Settings, Sales Process.
Locate Standard Sales Process and the Sales Phases included in that Sales Process.
In Floify:
Go to Company Dashboard, Company Settings.
Under Basic Settings, scroll down to Milestone Settings.
Select Manage Surefire Linking.
Add in the Surefire Sales Phases.
It is now time to link your Floify Milestones to your Surefire Sales Phases. This may require logging out of your account if you are still in the Company Dashboard, and logging back in.
Select Settings.
Select Milestones tab.
Click Manage Milestones.
The names of Surefire Sales Phases determine which in process email can be delivered to the borrower and other members of the deal. Review the content of these emails to be sure you select the correct linkage of Floify Milestones and Surefire Sales Phases.
To a link the Sales phases, select the Edit Milestone for any Milestone.
Link the Floify Milestones to the Surefire Sales Phases. The values for the Surefire Sales Phases that were input in Company Settings will appear in the Surefire Milestone dropdown.
Select Save.
Once all of the Milestones and Sales Phases you want are linked, then you're all set.
If you change the names of Sales Phases in Surefire the name will also need to be changed in Floify.
General Information
A data upload job will include details such as:
Who created the job
Who the job is assigned to The job name
Whether the job is initiated manually or via API Whether the upload is for User or Contact Records
The unique identifier for the data field map that's to be used and applied during this upload, called a "Mapping Tag" a json/xlsx/csv file containing the data objects that are to be imported.
Once the integration is fully established, then Surefire will receive new contacts from Floify, and either the Source field of the contact or a Tag can be added to the contact to denote that the contact was delivered by Floify.

In the Add Integration window, select Facebook.
Select Login to Facebook.
Enter your Facebook credentials.
If you have two-factor authentication turned on you may see an additional screen. Enter the code that Facebook texts you or authorize Surefire 's connection to Facebook from the Facebook App.
After successful Facebook account login, you will be prompted to select your Facebook pages.
Select all pages available for Facebook to start the integration.
Selecting all available pages does not start posting to all pages, only the specific pages selected for deployment will receive posts. If any available pages are left unselected, Facebook will not allow successful posting to any Facebook page via Surefire.
Select Yes to all settings to integrate properly.
This configures and confirms what Facebook details are visible in Surefire.
Click Done.
A confirmation screen appears verifying that you are now linked.
Select OK.
Now you can post from Surefire to this business page when deploying social media content.
Review Build an Audience for a Deployment for additional information.

Integrations
Integrate with Product and Pricing Engine (PPE)
ICE PPE Single Property Site
PPE Single Property Site
You can manage Single Property Site (SPS) Loan Programs by completing the following steps.
Go to Marketing, Single Property Sites.
Select the Program Settings tab.
Complete the following three elements on the in Program Settings : Program Categories - Individual Loan Programs must belong to a Program Category. For example, a company could have categories for 30-year, FHA, VA, and Jumbo. You can view these as broad categories of different loan types with underlying specific Loan Programs.
Review Create a Loan Program Category for additional information. Loan Programs - Within a Program Category, an admin can create and edit individual Loan Programs. These are for more specific types of loans than the broader Program Category. For example, for a 30 Year category, you could include programs such as 30-Year Fixed 5% Down, 30-Year Fixed 10% Down, 30-Year Fixed 15% Down, and 30-Year Fixed 20% Down. Once you create the Loan Programs, you can edit the attributes of the program (e.g., Rate, Term, Taxes, etc.) and adjust the rate by state.
Review Create a New Loan Program for additional information.
Program Groups
(Personal and Company) - Once a set of Loan Programs are created, you have the option to create your own Program Groups (or containers), with up to four programs. You apply the Program Group to a SPS and the group of programs is displayed in the Rate Table of the listing's Single Property Site Flyer.
Review Set the Default Loan Program Group for additional information.
Select Add Program on the Company Group Setup page, to Add Loan Programs to a group.
Create a Single Property Site
Select the Listing tab.
Click the Add New Listing button.
Set up a new listing by completing each section in the workflow and the related steps. 1 - Property - In the Property tab enter the MLS ID for the listing. By entering a valid MLS ID, you will be able to automatically pull in all of the information for the listing. If the MLS ID is not found, you will be able to manually enter the property information.
2 - Photos
- Surefire automatically pulls photos that are available from MLS. However, you can choose to remove any existing images or upload your own photos.
3 - Partner - Select which Surefire User is the Loan Officer for this listing (the currently logged in user appears as the default selection). It is this Surefire User's Contacts that will be listed as available selections for this listing's Co-brand partner. Select and define Co- brand Partner or if it is an FSBO property, choose the contact.
4 - Programs - In the Programs tab you will select from Your Group list and Rate Scenario created previously. This will return pricing results from your PPE system and allow you to select which products are displayed on the Single Property Site. 5 - Settings - Your default settings appear here and will apply to this listing.
Select Save and Publish.
Review View and Manage Single Property Sites (SPS) for additional information such as configure company settings, setup branch and licensing information, set default loan programs, set your brand and theme colors, manage layouts etc.

Example of a Single Property Site Flyer:

Configure Custom Rules
Go to CRM Settings, Custom Rules.
Select Create Rule.
Example Configuration: This rule fires when the Closing Date or Estimated Closing Date is 10 days from today. The first action updates the custom Closing Date field from the loan/deal record’s Estimated Closing Date or Closing Date (can use either) field. The second action is performed 1 minute later to send the contact data to OneSource via webhook.
Complete Rule Actions as applicable.
Examples:
Immediately update contact data (populate custom contact field with Closing Date)
After 1 min send data via webhook
Immediately send [Name of your new email collection created previously] to Borrower and CoBorrower (optional)
Select Apply.

Integrations
Integrate with Velocify
Integrate with Velocify Surefire integration with Velocify provides multiple features in Velocify (standalone) and in Encompass on the web interface Prospects tab.
Between Surefire and Velocify bidirectional data integration occurs and provides the following:
When turned on, Surefire can be configured to send contact records and updates to Velocify to be worked in Priority View or Normal View Surefire continues to send marketing and campaign related changes to the record; all typical lead fields in Surefire are locked
Velocify users can manage Surefire leads alongside their other Velocify leads
Velocify communicates changes in the lead record back to Surefire Surefire retrieves the latest version of the lead record to update the contact record
You can use Surefire fields in Velocify User Interface and APIs:
Velocify workflow, prioritization views and distribution have been optimized to include Surefire fields Surefire fields are available for use with lead forms, communications (Dial IQ, Email and SMS), templates, duplicate management, reporting and administration settings
A Hotlist feature (pre-packaged lists, campaigns, and campaign events) that uses Surefire 's fields is available in Normal View
Duplicate management logic accounts for Surefire leads and prevents creating duplicates

Integrations
Configure Webhook
This feature allows a user to push a contact's information directly to another source. The source is specified as a URL since this is an HTTP request. The receiving server will need to be configured appropriately, and the data pushed will be in JSON format. This function is completed by an admin.
To configuring the Webhook feature:
Go to CRM Settings, Webhooks.
Select Configure your company's webhook now.
By default, the Webhook feature is Disabled. To turn on the feature, it must first be configured.
Complete the following fields: Config 1 - you can configure a total of three webhook configurations.
Click the plus sign to add Config 2 & 3. Enabled - turns on the Webhook Config Name - enter a configuration name Request Method - POST method is the only request method option Webhook URL to be called - enter the destination URL of the webhook Authentication Mode - select from the list: Query Token - Requires query token and param name and value Request Header Token - Requires header key name and value Basic Authentication - Requires username and password
Authentication Modes and Values are what validate the incoming data for the recipient server. If you are unsure what to place here, please contact the recipient server manager.
Select Test.
Once the Test is selected, a sample set of data is sent to the recipient server, and an active window opens in the Webhook feature displaying a response from the recipient server if it has been established.
If any errors occur, ensure that configurations on both the recipient server and the Webhook feature are accurate.
Select Enable QOS Alert on Failure - sends email alerts when a webhook fails. Email Recipient - enter an email address Email Subject - enter an email subject
Click Save Webhook Config.
In the Contact Webhook Button Label, enter text that will appear on the button that users select in the CRM.
Example: If contacts are sent to Encompass, the button could display
Push Contact to Encompass
Select Show UI Button.
Select Save UI Setting.
The right-hand side of this panel displays all contact fields that can be sent to the recipient server, as well as a tab with sample JSON. (Example Contact Data)
User Identifiers included in the Webhook are as follows:
Copy
"user": {
"fullName": "Phil Lender",
"username": "integrationtestingsetupseat",
"id": "bK7BU3", "email": " none@topofmindlending.com
",
"companyName": "Top of Mind Lending",
"syncIdentifier": "342188"
Additional Testing
Once initial tests have been run, it is now possible to push an actual contact. First, find the contact to push using the Webhook feature. There are two areas where the button display.
Click where contacts are initially listed upon search.
Click on the contact profile itself.
The push should be relatively immediate, and a log of what contacts have been pushed can be found in the Webhook configuration area.
You can click the Inspect Request button to open a window displaying JSON sent to the recipient server, as well as the recipient server's response.

Zapier is a popular SaaS tool that lets users easily connect and automate the apps they use. Users can utilize integrations that can connect with hundreds of apps including Surefire CRM. Review www.zapier.com for additional information.
Connect Surefire to Zapier
In this section, we explain how to connect the Surefire CRM account to your Zapier account, opening up the power of hundreds of public API connections.
Enter your Zapier user credentials in www.zapier.com. Alternatively, create an account.
In the Search field, type Surefire CRM.
Click Surefire CRM icon to select it as the app you want to connect to your Zapier account.
Obtain the Zapier API Key from Surefire. Navigate to My Account, My Profile, Integrations, Zapier.
Copy
My API Key.
Paste the Zapier API key into the API Key field.
Click Yes, Continue. button.
Your accounts are now connected.
Zaps, Triggers, and Actions
Before you start using Zapier to automate certain Surefire tasks, it's important to understand some of Zapier's basic concepts.
Zaps
A Zap is an automated workflow between your apps. For example, you may have a Zap that creates new Surefire contacts from labeled emails in Gmail and another Zap that creates Surefire contacts from new Zillow agent hub contacts.
Zaps consist of at least two parts: a Trigger and one or more Actions.
Triggers
A Trigger is an event in an app that starts the Zap. Once you set up a Zap, Zapier will monitor the app for that event. For a "Save Gmail attachments to Dropbox" Zap, for example, you can receive a lot of emails through your Gmail account, but the Zap is not triggered until an email that contains an attachment is received.
Actions
Action is the event that completes the Zap. For the Gmail to Dropbox Zap example, the action is saving the Gmail attachment to Dropbox.
Currently, the only action available for Zapier to take in Surefire is the creation of a new Contact Record.
Review Contacts for additional information.
Review Zapier's Learning Center for additional information.
Create Zaps for Surefire Currently the only action available for Zapier to take in Surefire is the creation of a new Contact.
Nevertheless, there are still several opportunities to use Zapier. For example, you could create Zaps that create new Surefire contacts: from labeled emails in Gmail for Leads generated from Facebook Lead Advertisements whenever Lead Generation Forms are filled out on LinkedIn for any attendees that are added to an event you've set up in Eventbrite for any new Zillow lender hub contacts that get created. when new rows are added to a Google spreadsheet
Use Case
Let's take a closer look at that last example listed above: Create new Surefire contacts when new rows are added to a Google spreadsheet.
To illustrate how this zap might work, let's say you have a Google sheet called "Realtor Partners" where you or members of your team keep and add contact and other details about Realtors you work with. Like most Contacts spreadsheets, you have a column corresponding to each Contact attribute (First Name, Last Name, Mobile Phone number, etc).
You could create a Zap whose trigger is the addition of a new row to this spreadsheet. You would then in turn configure the Zap to map the values entered into given columns of any new row to correspond to fields in a Contact Record in Surefire.
Then, whenever a new row is appended to your Google sheet, Zapier would be triggered and would run your Zap to create a corresponding Contact Record in Surefire.

You only need to map this field if you are a Surefire administrator distributing leads for the entire company/branch. If you are an individual user, then no need to map this field and all leads will be added to your account directly. Integrations
Integrate with Zapier
Sync with Zapier, No Name Leads
If you automated importing your Zillow leads to Surefire using Zapier you may see an error notification on your Zap Alert.
This occurs because Zillow leads does not require their lead capture form to enter a first or last name. However, first and last names are required fields in Surefire, and first name is critical for marketing automation.
The video below shows you how to use Zapier along with the Surefire rules engine to overcome this challenge, make use of the best data you have, and still maintain full marketing automation.
