Marketing
View and Manage Single Property Sites (SPS)
Manage SPS Default Disclaimers
Administrators can add, edit or delete the contents of the Disclaimers that are made available for selection by Standard Users for inclusion on their Single Property Sites.
Disclaimers are organized into 4 categories:
Loan Comparison Disclaimers
Mortgage Pro Disclaimers
Co-Brand Partner Disclaimers
Flyer Disclaimers
For each Disclaimer category, Administrators can add and edit a default disclaimer (i.e. the disclaimer that will be presented to Standard Users as a default selection).
Administrators can also add additional, alternate disclaimers (i.e. disclaimers that Standard Users will be given the option to actively select instead of the default disclaimer).
When present, alternate disclaimers can be "promoted" by Administrators so that they become a default disclaimer. When this is done, the previous default disclaimer is demoted and becomes simply another alternate disclaimer.
Add a Disclaimer
Go to Marketing, Single Property Sites.
Select Company Settings.
Select + sign to expand the Company Disclaimers Settings section.
Select Add New.
Use the text editor's tools to edit your Disclaimer Text much like you would a document in a word processing software.
The options to use Merge Fields for dynamic values such as Company License, Company State License or User State License
The text editor also includes styles formatting (bold, italic, underline), web resource linking, a safe undo function, a built-in spell checker, paste-from-Word and other common HTML formatting tools.
Disclaimers can be a maximum of 400 characters in length.
Select Save.
Edit a Disclaimer
Go to Marketing, Single Property Sites.
Select Company Settings
Select + sign to expand the Company Disclaimers Settings section.
Scroll down to the Disclaimer you want to edit and click the Edit Button.
A text editor pop-up window with the disclaimer's contents is displayed.
Use the text editor's tools to edit your Disclaimer Text much like you would a document in a word processing software (e.g Microsoft Word).
The options to use Merge Fields for dynamic values such as Company License, Company State License or User State License
The text editor also includes styles formatting (bold, italic, underline), web resource linking, a safe undo function, a built-in spell checker, paste-from-Word and other common HTML formatting tools.
Disclaimers can be a maximum of 400 characters in length.
Select Save.
Select X button to be returned to the Company Settings page.
Delete a Disclaimer
To delete a Default Disclaimer, you must promote an alternate disclaimer so that it becomes the default or create and then promote an alternate disclaimer if no alternate exists. Default Disclaimers cannot be deleted. This is because the system does not allow there to be null content for any disclaimer category.
Go to Marketing, Single Property Sites
Select Company Settings.
Select + sign to expand the Company Disclaimers Settings section.
Scroll down to the Disclaimer you want to edit and click the Delete Button.
Select OK in the confirmation pop-up window.
Set a New Default Disclaimer
Go to Marketing, Single Property Site.
Select Company Settings.
Select + sign to expand the Company Disclaimers Settings section.
Scroll down to the Alternate Disclaimer you want to promote and click the Make Default Button.
The Alternate Disclaimer becomes a default disclaimer for the Disclaimer Category it's in and the formerly Default Disclaimer is demoted and becomes simply another Alternate Disclaimer.
Add Additional Disclaimers for a Selection
This is an Administrators Only function. Administrators can add additional Disclaimers for Users to choose from when they are creating Single Property Sites.
Go to Marketing, Single Property Sites.
Select My Settings
Select + sign to expand the Disclaimers Settings section. Add, Edit, Delete or Promote the Disclaimer(s) of your choice.
Changes made are reflected in the Disclaimer selections made available to you when you create a Single Property Site.
Changes made here are not reflected in the Disclaimer selections made available to Standard Users when they create a Single Property Site.

Marketing
View and Manage Single Property Sites (SPS)
Create a New Loan Program
To create, edit and view Loan Programs, from the Single Property Site main page, go to Program Settings tab in the top menu and then click on Program Setup.
You are presented with a view of all of your Loan Programs organized by Loan Category.
You can edit/change the rate of the loan program by clicking the green edit button, scrolling to program rate and making your changes in the Program Rate field and Save.
To edit many program rates quickly you can use the drop-down under Base Program Rate.
If you are integrated with Optimal Blue, these lists are only visible to Admins.
In a Program Category, admins can create and edit individual Loan Programs. These are for more specific types of loans than the broader Category.
In the example above, for the 20 Year Category, you could include Loan Programs such as:
20 Yr Fixed 10% Down
20 Yr Fixed 15% Down
20 Yr Fixed 20% Down
You can perform the following actions with a Loan Program:
Create a New Loan Program
Edit & Delete Program
Adjust Rates by State
Set Base Program Rates
Set Points/Origination Fee
Create a Loan Program
To create a Loan Program, click the Create New Program button under the appropriate Category. If your category is not listed, you will need to first Create a Loan Category.
Once you create a Program, you’ll enter your Program Details. This consists of a set of dynamic fields that will pre-populate as well as a set of static fields that perform calculations based upon what numbers you enter into the dynamic fields.
You also have the option to make all field values a manually entered value by selecting the Use manual rates checkbox.
Loan Programs are divided into the following sections with the corresponding dynamic fields for you to enter:
Loan Program & Program Group Setup
Sale Price
Taxes
Condo/HOA Fee
Down Payment
Down Payment %
Mortgage
UFMIP/SP PMI/VAFF
Program Rate
Term in Months
Monthly Expenses
Property Insurance (monthly)
MI or PMI
Closing Costs
1st Loan Avg. Est. Costs @
Points
Other (i.e. Seller Credit, etc.)
Lender Credit
Use the toggles to choose whether any of the below values appear as dollar or percentage values.
Use the toggles to choose whether any of the below values appear as dollar or percentage values
APR
Continuance for MI
Pre-Paid Expenses
Days of Pre-paid Interest
Months of Taxes @
Months of Insurance @
Months of HOA/Condo Fee
Months of PMI
Clone, Edit & Delete Loan Programs
Select Clone next to any Loan Program to append an additional entry in the table (directly below that Loan Program) with the same info, you can then use the drop-down menus to alter the Rate and/or Points/Origination Fee, not to mention all of the other Loan Program details as described in the previous section of this article.
Select Edit next to any Loan Program to change any of the loan variables.
If you select Delete and confirm, you will completely remove the Loan Program from your Single Property platform.
If the Loan Program belongs to any Groups, it will be removed from the Group. This will carry over to Single Property sites. So if the Group containing the deleted Loan Program is already actively applied to a Listing, the deleted Loan Program will be removed from the Rate Table the next time that a Single Property Site Flyer is generated.

Manage SPS Loan Programs
Go to Marketing, Single Property Sites.
Select Program Settings tab.
Modify the Loan Programs. The Program Settings section is divided into four areas:
Categories
Program Setup
My Group Setup
Company Group Setup
Start in the Program Setup section:
Program Settings are structured using a simple system composed of three elements:
Categories
Loan Programs
Program Groups (Personal and Company)
Program Categories
Individual Loan Programs must belong to a Program Category. For example, a company could have Categories for:
30-year
FHA
VA
Jumbo
Think of these as the broad categories of different loan types of which there are then more underlying specific Loan Programs. Click here to learn how to Create a Loan Program Category.
Loan Programs
In the Program Category, admins can create and edit individual Loan Programs. These are for more specific types of loans than the broader Category.
In the example above, for the 30 Year category, you could include Loan Programs such as:
30-Year Fixed 5% Down
30-Year Fixed 10% Down
30-Year Fixed 15% Down
30-Year Fixed 20% Down
After you create them, you can edit the attributes of Loan Programs (e.g. Rate, Term, Taxes, etc.) as well as adjust the rate by state.
Program Group Setup
Once a set of Loan Programs are created, you have the option to create your own Program Group(s), which is a collection of up to four Loan Programs. The group is only the container, to add loan programs to a group - from company group set up, select Add Program.
Apply the Program Group to a Single Property Site and the Program Group of Loan Programs appears in the Rate Table of the Listing's Single Property Site Flyer.

View and Manage Single Property Sites (SPS)
Continuance for MI in the Program Edit Screen in SPS Continuance for MI in the Program Edit Screen in SPS When editing a Program in Single Property Sites (SPS) you will a see a field called Continuance for MI.
This field affects your APR, it defaults to 11. You can change it if you'd like. We find that 11 gives the most accurate APR. If editing this field, we recommend that you have a side-by-side loan comparison with your LOS software to ensure that your APR stays within the set tolerance.

Marketing
View and Manage Single Property Sites (SPS)
Create a Single Property Site
Create SPS - Enter Property Info
In the Property tab enter the MLS ID for the listing. By entering a valid MLS ID, you will be able to automatically pull in all of the information for the listing. Finding an MLS ID# - Use https://www.realtor.com/ to find and copy a valid MLS ID or ask your referral partner for the ID. Enter the MLS ID# - Type or paste the MLS ID you copied and use the drop-down to select the property State and then click the Search button.
The Single Property Site system supports Multiple Listing Services nationwide, but occasionally you will find that your valid MLS ID isn’t found.
If this happens, you can still create a Single Property Site quickly and easily.
From Listings, Add Listing.
Key in the property information
Upload your Property Photos in Workflow 2
Add your Partner in Workflow 3
Select your Loan Programs in Workflow 4
Adjust your Settings in Workflow 5
Select Save & Publish.
For more information about integrating partners with our platform review Set up Your Broker Partner on ListHub
Property Details are populated into the various fields. Each field's data is editable. If you find information missing such as taxes, stories, etc. you ccan make adjustments as needed.
Select Save & Continue.
Additional Information
For the Title, use a short catchy description highlighting the most important and exciting thing(s) about the property. Adorable bungalow, steps from the beach!, Modern condo with city view, or Rare single level rambler!
Property Description (Short) is how the description will appear on a flyer. Take note of the character limit remaining. You cannot Save if you exceed the limit.
Property Description (Long) is what will appear on the website. Here you have the liberty of a more detailed description.
Annual R.E. Taxes must be greater than zero if they do not populate (which happens sometimes), so use an estimation or look up the property on the county auditors site and fill in the correct number.

View and Manage Single Property Sites (SPS)
Create a Single Property Site
Create SPS - Upload Photo
In the next step select Photos to include for the Listing. The system automatically pulls whatever Photos are available from the MLS; however, you can choose to remove any existing images and/or upload your own photos.
The MLS ID and State will have returned a max of 30 photos associated with the property.
(Optional) Add a video tour of the property by pasting the Vimeo or YouTube URL.
(Optional) Add a Matterport 3D tour.
Select Show All Photos to see the entire set of property photos.
You can change the Primary Image of the Single Property Site, the large, main image set as the background at the top of the website, drag the image from the grid and drop it below where it says Primary Image. Delete a Photo, click on the image to select the Photo. Press and hold the Shift Key as you click on an image to select more than one Photo. Re-click a Photo to deselect it. Click Delete Photos and confirm to permanently delete the selected Photos.
If you want to upload a custom image. Select Browse Photos and upload an image from your desktop.
Once the upload is completed, the image will appear in the group of All Photos.
Select Save & Continue.
Edit Photos for a Previously Created Single Property Site
If a Single Property Site has already been created and the Photos Section now needs to be edited, use the Refresh Photos button available.
Below are some guidelines around what to expect when using the Refresh Photos button.
If the created site previously had no photos - if no photos are available still, then you will get a message saying so and nothing will change with the site.
If there are photos now available, they will be uploaded - If at any point the cancel refresh button is pushed, then nothing will change.
If the created site had photos originally, upon hitting the Refresh Photos:
You will get the option to replace all the original photos with the new ones available.
If there are no new photos available, then a message will appear saying no images were found and nothing will change.
If there are manually uploaded photos prior to refreshing, then those too will be removed and replaced during the refresh process should new photos be available.
If the entire site was manually created and photos were manually uploaded, then hitting the Refresh Photos button
All photos will be retained.
If the MLS # is queried during the edit prior to hitting the refresh button and photos are found, then you will get a message saying that photos are available. You are then given the option to choose. If you choose to upload the new photos, then all manually uploaded photos will be removed and replaced.

Create a Single Property Flyer
You can create a PDF Flyer version of a Single Property Site (SPS). Similar to the website, the flyer will contain:
Listing Photos
Listing Description
Loan Officer Contact Info
Co-Brand Partner Contact Info

Alternatively, you can also create a flyer directly from the site. Open the site by clicking on the site's image, locate the Share icons and select.
QR Code
Single Property Site flyers will automatically include a QR code located either at the top right or left corner of the flyer. This QR code when scanned will take you to the URL for the website listing of the property in the flyer.
The inclusion of a QR Code on Single Property Site flyers can be managed on a company wide bases in Company Settings, Manage Flyers.
No QR code will be applied Single Property Site flyers if the Disable sites and only use flyers setting is checked, as there has been no property website created and available to link.

Add Tracking Code to SPS Add Tracking Code to SPS It is possible to add a 3rd party tracker to your Single Property Sites (SPS) such as Facebook Pixel, Google Analytics, or other tracking code.
In Company Settings locate the Tracking Code
Select to expand it.
Obtain the code from the 3rd party and paste it in the box.
Select Save Settings.
The code is applied to all sites across your entire organization. Users have this setting as well if they have their own tracking code.
Under My Settings expand the tracking code box and paste in the tracking code. The sites support both the company tracking code and the user tracking code at once.

Pricing information is only generated for states the user is licensed in.

Enter data that you have for a given borrower scenario, e.g. Loan Types, Loan Terms, etc.
Any Custom Fields associated with your Optimal Blue Pricing Channel are displayed in the lower right-hand corner of the screen.
Select Save Scenario.

Navigate to the folder that contains the Rate Scenario you want to review.
Select the applicable Rate Scenario with the day's pricing details.
A list of products for the Rate Scenario you selected (Products List for [Rate Scenario]) displays.

Marketing
Landing Pages
A Landing Page is a stand-alone webpage created specifically for the purposes of marketing or the display of content-based materials. You can create a landing page by navigating to Marketing and then clicking Landing Pages.

Marketing
Landing Pages
Professional Pages
A professional landing page, also known as a vanity page, is a stand-alone web page. It is used as a method to introduce a Loan Officer and provide links to apply for a loan, contact the loan officer via phone or email, and capture leads via an embedded form.
A template is available in Surefire that can be used to create a web page and corresponding URL. The template pulls data from the Company and User profiles in Surefire to create the web page.
The URL can then be added to emails, text, and social collections.
Each user has a unique link that requires a user profile in Surefire to populate user information including:
Company Name, logo, and website
Loan Officer contact information, social media links, NMLS ID, and photo
Application URL for Apply Now link
Bio Block
Contact Me
You can customize of the professional page.
Complete Company and User Profiles
Your Professional Page needs the following information in your Surefire Company & User Profiles.
Required fields are annotated with an *. All others are optional.
Company
My Company, Company Info, Edit Company, can only be edited by Admins:
Company Logo*
Company Website (this is required for your logo to appear)
Company Name
Create user profiles, if needed
Review Edit User Profile for additional information.
User My Account, My Profile:
First and Last Name*
Title
NMLS id located under My Account, My Profile, Licensing tab
Application URL this is required for Apply Now button to appear
User Social Media Links, only links populated will display the social icon. Only Facebook, LinkedIn, and Instagram are supported.
User Email
User Primary Phone
User Mobile Phone
User Bio Block
Review Edit User Signature Block for additional information.
Company Color is color 0 from the Company Color Theme. Located under
My Company, Company Info, Settings, Color Theme.
Generate the Link
The Professional Page template is located in the Public folder under Marketing, Landing Pages. If you do not have access to the Public folder, contact your Company’s Surefire administrator to ask about cloning options.
Admins, the public folder is available to users by default. If you have hidden the folder, you’ll need to clone the Professional Page to make it available to users.
Users can generate their link from the template itself or clone the page (if permission is granted) and make edits before obtaining their link. To generate the link, click, select Get My Link.
Add the Unique Link to a Collection
You can add the unique link, once copied, to a location such as an email. Surefire also allows you to insert your Professional Page in a collection from the Media Library.

Marketing
Landing Pages
Add a Content Block
Each element of your Landing Page is contained in a Content Block. The content block can contain all the building blocks of a simple web page such as Text, Buttons, Dividers, Tables etc.
Content Blocks can be structured in multiple ways.
Each Content Block is labeled, and those labels are, unless otherwise specified, displayed across the top of a published Landing Page as Menu items. Clicking on a menu item will scroll the page down to the corresponding Content Block.
Blocks can be added, formatted and moved around your page using the Style Panel.
To Add Content to a Content Block, select the Click to edit button to bring up a menu of the following options: Structure - Choose the column structure for your content block row.
Elements Text Editor - Insert a block of text. The block can include a table, images, links, as well as dynamically populated Surefire fields such as Recipient Names or Addresses. Additionally, you can Select the HTML button on the Edit Menu to bring up an HTML Source Code pop up where you can paste in any kind of HTML that you'd like rendered on your Landing Page. Divider - Add a horizontal line to visually separate sections or elements of your Landing Page. Image - Add an image to your page: Either choose an image that's already in your Surefire Media Library or upload a new one. Uploaded images are added to your Surefire Media Library. Empty Content - Insert a horizontal bar of white space into your Landing Page in order to visually separate sections or elements of your Landing Page.
Social Bar
-The Social bar is an option for a Content Block in a Landing Page. Landing Pages that are associated with Permalinks will not have a Like button option but will have social media sharing options, including Facebook, Twitter, Google+, LinkedIn, Pinterest, and email. Landing Pages without Permalinks will have both thumbs up and social media sharing options. Power Video Player - Only available to companies with Power Video subscription. Forms - Embed a Form as an element in your Landing Page. A Form's Title will automatically be inserted above the form as its own content block. If you wish, you can choose to hide the Title when you Style your Landing Page.
Dynamic Videos -
Embed a preconfigured video, some of whose text content can be dynamically personalized by associating it with Roles in Surefire. Interactives - Embed an interactive. Choose to use one from the Public folder or one of your own.

Marketing
Landing Pages
Style a Content Block
The Style Panel is where you can organize and design your Landing Page, Content Blocks. Click on the Style Panel to bring up the Content Block Customizer Panel and then click on a Content Block. That Content Block's style attributes are now displayed and can be adjusted in the Content Block Customizer Panel.
Content Block Customizer Panel
The top half of the Panel includes several options to customize your Content Block. Switch Between Content Blocks - Use the drop down menu at the top of the Panel to select which Content Block you want your customizations to apply to.
Select X to disassociate the Panel from any Content Blocks. Add/Remove Content Blocks - Select + to select Add a Content Block from the list.
Select Delete Content Block button to delete whichever Content Block is currently selected in the Content Block drop down selection menu.
Menu Label -
This is where you edit the Label for a Content Block. In addition to identifying a Content Block for the purpose of Landing Page organization and editing, a Content Block's Label will also be displayed at the top of a published Landing Page as a Menu item. Clicking on a menu item will scroll the page down to the corresponding Content Block. Hide from Menu - When you set this to YES, a link to whichever Content Block is currently selected in the Content Block drop down selection menu will not appear as a click-able menu item at the top of the Landing Page. Move Up/Down - Each Content Block spans the entire width of a Landing Page. Thus Content Blocks are arranged on a Landing Page, one-on-top-of-the-other, from the top of the Landing Page to bottom.
You can move whichever Content Block is currently selected in the Content Block drop down selection menu up or down through this arrangement using the Move arrow buttons.
Basic Settings
On the Basic Settings tab, at the bottom of the Panel, you can specify the design of each Content Block. Alignment - Choose how and where in the Content Block's content (labelled as "Element or Object" in the figure below) is displayed. Choose from Left Aligned (i.e. content starts at the left-most margin), Centered (i.e. centers content on the middle margin of the Content Block), or Right Justified (i.e. content starts a the right-most margin).
Select auto to clear any selections you've made and revert to system defaults.
Padding -
Padding defines the amount of space around content (labelled as "Element or Object" in the figure below) in a Content Block that's kept reserved as empty.
In the Landing Page builder, Padding can be measured in pixels, as a percentage of the width of the entire Content Block including its border or as "em," which is a unit relative to the font-size of the Content Block (e.g. 2em means 2 times the size of the current font).
Select auto to clear any selections you've made and revert to system defaults. Margin - The Margin defines the amount of space, measured inward from the edge of the Content Block, that's kept reserved as empty.
In the Landing Page builder, Margin can be measured in pixels, as a percentage of the width of the entire Content Block including its border or as "em," which is a unit relative to the font-size of the Content Block (e.g. 2em means 2 times the size of the current font)
Select auto to clear any selections you've made and revert to system defaults. Border - The Border describes the outside edge of the Content Block. Content Block Borders can be rendered in several different styles such as solid lines, dotted lines, double lines or inset/outset (which uses color hues and angles to create a 3D effect) among others.
Border widths are measured in pixels.
Select None to clear any selections you've made and revert to system defaults. Border Radius - The Border Radius property is used to add rounded corners to a Content Block. If you specify only one value for the border-radius property, this radius will be applied to all four corners. Alternatively, you can specify each corner separately.

Marketing
Landing Pages
Create a Landing Page
You can create a Landing Page in Surefire to host a Form for lead generation, surveys, or any other marketing purposes.
Choose to use the native WYSIWYG editor to build and design your Landing Page, or import HTML you have designed offsite.
To create a Landing Page:
Go to Marketing, Landing Pages.
Select + Create button near the top of the page.
In the What do you want to create? screen, select New Landing Page..
Enter a Name and Description for your Landing Page.
Select a Folder from the list.
This indicates the Surefire Users that are able to access this Landing Page by selecting where in the Media Library you want to save it.
In the Landing Page Builder screen tools used to create landing page including:
Page Settings
Page Style
New Content Block
Style Panel
Page Settings
Enter the basic details that describe and identify your Landing Page both as a Surefire media asset and as a Web Page.
General Landing Page Name - The Landing Page's name as it appears in Surefire Media Library. Public Page Title - Page Title is a required field. It defines a title in the browser toolbar, provides a title for the page when it is added to favorites, displays a title for the page in search engine results, and is the primary title in social postings. Public Page Description - A Page Description is also a required field. It provides further information on the purpose of the landing page. This information will be shown below the Title in social postings. Public OG Image URL - This is the image asset that will be used in conjunction with the posting. Click on the Select from Media Library button and you are presented with the asset library to choose your image asset. Layout - Select a pre-designed Header (e.g. a logo) and/or Footer (e.g. Contact Info and other small print) to appear on your Landing Page.
You cannot edit this from the Landing Page editor; it can only be modified as a Layout. Media Library Tags - Tags are unique identifiers that can be added, like labels, in order to further categorize your Landing Page in Surefire. Tagging lets you easily sort, filter, and associate your Landing Page with campaigns or other specific topics and actions. A Landing Page can have multiple Tags. Enable Social Share Bar - When turned on, it provides a bar of social links to allow for the sharing of content. Favicon URL - This is the image asset that will be used to populate the favicon image in the browser tab. Click on the Select from Media Library button, and you will be presented with the asset library to choose your image asset.
Permalink (if applicable)
Domain
Permalink Path
Default Fallback User
This is a required field.
Meta Tags -
Add Meta Tags to your Landing Page so that your Landing Page can be linked back to from social media postings. Meta Tag names will be prefixed with Surefire.
Integrations Google Analytics Tracking ID - A Google Analytics code is provided by Google and is used by marketers to track web page visits. FB Pixel Tracking ID - A Facebook Pixel is a tracking code provided to you by Facebook. It's used by advertisers to increase the effectiveness of their ads and their budget.
This only applies to paid Facebook ads and is not used for organic Facebook postings.
Page Style -
This is where you select the overall look and feel for your Landing Page that spans across all of its elements. New Content Block - each element of your Landing Page will be contained in a Content Block, which can contain Text, Buttons, Dividers, Tables, Dynamic or Static video, Forms... pretty much most of the building blocks of a simple web page. Style Panel - Use this button to toggle whether the Style Panel is visible or not.
The Style panel is where, among other actions, you move Content Block placements up or down on your Landing Page as well as where you style your Content Blocks' alignment, padding, margin, and border.
Preview, Save and Publish/Unpublish Save - Click the Save button in the upper right of the screen to save your work at any time. Preview - Click the Preview button to see what your Landing Page, in its current state, will look like when published. Publish/Unpublish - From drop-down menu next to "Status" in the upper right of the screen, select Publish to make your Landing Page available as an embeddable link in other Surefire media such as emails.
When you select Unpublished, anyone clicking on a previously embedded link to this Landing Page will be taken to a Page Does Not Exist page.

Marketing
Landing Pages
Style a Landing Page
The Page Style menu on the Landing Page lets you define the overall look and feel across all of your Landing Page's elements.
Background Background Color - Choose a color for your Landing Page's background by either selecting from the color palette or entering an HTML hex code.
Background Image
-Assign an image as the background to your page. You have two options for doing this:
Use Existing Online Image -For images already hosted online, paste their file path URL and hit Apply.
Select from Media Library - Click the button to choose an image that's already in your Surefire Media Library. Navigate within your Library to find the image you want, click the check box next to it and then hit Apply. You can also choose to Upload a New Image to your Library
Apply up to five external CSSs (Cascading Style Sheets) to your Landing Page, identified by their URLs. CSS describes how HTML elements are to be displayed on screen by defining styles for your web pages, including the design, layout and variations in display for different devices and screen sizes.
CSS
Apply up to five external CSSs (Cascading Style Sheets) to your Landing Page, identified by their URLs. CSS describes how HTML elements are to be displayed on screen by defining styles for your web pages, including the design, layout and variations in display for different devices and screen sizes.
You should only adjust this setting if you are a qualified HTML developer.
CSS Editor
Use CSS syntax to add custom styles in addition to any CSS you've applied to the page.
You should only adjust this setting if you are a qualified HTML developer.
Menu Editor
You can style how the Menus look on your Landing Page. You can specify the following attributes: Background Image - Select an image as the background of your menu. This will override any color chosen. Background Image Fill Type - Select between Cover Fill and Stretch Fill.
Cover Fill - uses the actual size of the image with the upper portion of the image flush to the top and the rest only partially visible.
Stretch Fill - stretches out the dimensions of a smaller image to fill the menu width. If using an image, it is best to use something that is smaller and evokes a pattern. Background Color - Select a color or enter an HTML hex code for the background if you don't want to use an image. Link Color - Select a color or enter an HTML hex code for the text links in the menu. Border Color - Select a color or enter an HTML hex code for the bottom border of the menu. Border Width - Select a pixel width for the menu border. This will default to 0px.
Content Block Menu Labels
-Click the tabs for each Content Block to set the Menu Name. Alternately, toggle the Hide from Displaying on Menu switch to Yes in order to remove the Content Block from the menu.
Forms Options
Each Form page in Surefire is given a Title. Choose whether this title is displayed on your Landing Page or not by setting this toggle selector.
Form Style Override
Forms are configured to have their own style attributes that are independent of any styles applied to the rest of the page by CSS. Use Form Style Override to adjust any of these styles in order to change how forms appear on your Landing Page.
You should only adjust this setting if you are a qualified HTML developer.

Marketing
Landing Pages
Your Homebuying Team In-Site
Your Homebuying Team In-Site Surefire 's Your Homebuying Team In-Site can be used as-is or can be personalized for your team. Without personalization, the In-Site provides a good overview of the roles of different team members. With personalization, it’s a great option for introducing your team members.
The In-Site has two landing page options – Dynamic and Permalink. Each is available in English or Spanish.
Your Homebuying Team Dynamic
Dynamic landing pages are available to send through email or text messaging only.
Surefire ’s Your Homebuying Team In-Site collection in the Public, In-Sites folder uses the dynamic landing page in the email and text message media types.
Populates photo, primary phone number and email address for Loan Officer, Buying Agent (called Real Estate Agent in the In-Site), Listing Agent and Processor of the recipient’s Primary Deal as noted in their Surefire contact record. See instructions below if you do not have photos of your deal team members.
If the recipient completes the form, their responses will automatically update their Surefire contact record.
Your Homebuying Team Permalink
Permalink landing pages can be sent through email, text messaging or social deployment.
Surefire ’s Your Homebuying Team In-Site collection in the Public, In-Sites folder uses the permalink landing page for the social deployment.
Populates Loan Officer’s photo, primary phone number, and email address.
Photos and contact information for other homebuying team members can be added manually. Instructions below. Added personalization of a permalink landing page is a good option for introducing your team members on social media or to recipients who do not yet have a deal.
If the contact form is returned, the response will create a new contact record in Surefire (following de-dupe policies set up by your company).
Manually add Team Members to your Homebuying Team Permalink Landing Page Clone the Y our Homebuying Team In-Site Permalink landing page in the Public, In-Sites folder.
Verify you are viewing Assets.
Select HTML button in the Landing Page Builder.
Press CTRL+F to initiate the Find function.
Enter a team member’s role name.
In the sample below, we searched attorney. You can locate the part of the code that describes the team member’s role. In the area just above the description, locate this line, marked in red below:
Copy
<div class=”image-area”> <img class=”no-picture” src=”#” /></div> Delete class="no-picture "
Replace the # with the URL of the team member’s picture.
You can get the URL by navigating to the team member’s contact record, right clicking on their image, and clicking on Copy Image Link or Copy Image Addres s, depending on your browser. If you do not have images in your contact records, skip this step.
Below the image line, locate the line that contains the team member’s contact information:
Copy
<div class=”contact-info empty”(Name) | (Phone) | (Email)</div> Delete the word empty after contact-info. Edit the remaining text to fill in name and contact information for your team member.
Save and preview to view the result:
Repeat the steps above for each team member you want to highlight.
If you don’t have images of your deal team members, you may want to adjust the code in the Your Homebuying Team Dynamic landing page. This will prevent some display oddities, particularly in mobile view.
Refer to the steps above to clone the Your Homebuying Team Dynamic landing page, navigate to the HTML source code and locate the section that applies to the team members normally included in the page but for whom you don’t have images either LO, Buying Agent, Listing Agent or Processor.
Locate the line of code that relates to the team member’s image, marked in red below:
Copy
&lt;div class="image-area"&gt;{{Loan - Buying Agent Image - Photo}}&lt;/div&gt;
Delete the merge field for the team member’s image. In this case, you’ll delete:
Copy
{{Loan – Buying Agent Image – Photo}}</div>. Insert: <img class= "no-picture" />

Marketing
Landing Pages
Insert Landing Page Link Into Email with the Classic Email Editor
Landing Pages are pages designed and configured in Surefire that you can direct your Contacts to for the purposes of introducing and publicizing your products and services.
Landing Pages can be reached by inserting a link into an email sent from Surefire.
To Insert a Landing Page in an Email:
Go to Marketing, Media Library.
Select a Content Collection that contains an email you want on insert a Landing Page link into Alternatively, you can Create an Email for a Content Collection.
Under the Content editing menu, select Insert Landing Page.
In the Insert Landing Page Link window, click Select Landing Page to choose your selected Landing Page from the asset browser.
Insert a Dynamic Landing Page
Select which Domain your page will be hosted on. An admin can configure multiple domains.
Enter what you want to appear as the hyperlinked Text in the email.
Alternatively, select a Link Image to appear instead of Text for the link.
Link Style is for CSS code that is used to set the font, size, shape and color of the link (e.g. a big, round, red button).
If link style CSS code is available with a landing page then this field will auto-fill that code. This is not a required field.
Image Style is for CSS code used to style the image used. If Image style CSS code is available with a landing page then this field will auto-fill that code. This is NOT a required field.
Choose if you want to apply URL shortener service (e.g. bit.ly).
Create Secure Links defaults to YES provides a higher level of security token to be used specifically when sensitive information might be shared through your landing page link.
You can also choose to have your landing page link expire at a certain timeframe. If you click YES to have it expire, you will then add the number of days if will remain active prior to expiring.
Insert a Permalink Landing Page
A Permalink Landing Page presents a more limited pop-up menu, as the domain link is set.
Enter what you want to appear as the hyperlinked Text in the email.
Alternatively, select a Link Image to appear instead of Text for the link.
Link Style is where CSS code is used to set the font, size, shape and color of the link (e.g. a big, round, red button).
If link style CSS code is available with a landing page, then this field will auto-fill that code. This is not a required field.
Permalink Landing Page are tied to a specific user, cannot include contact information or be used with contact-specific dynamic content. As such, the extra security options found for Dynamic Landing Pages are not included when inserting a Permalink Landing Page into an Email.
If you want your Landing Page to display a customized URL, you can adjust these options and settings under
Master Settings, Web Pages.

Marketing
Landing Pages
Dynamic vs. Permalink Landing Pages
Dynamic
The URL changes based on the contact it's sent to, this is called a PURL (or a personalized URL)
The URL is available via Email and Text Message.
Commonly used for the Journey To Your New Home series or Refinance Adventure, as these pages are personalized for the contact AND the User.
Permalink
This means the URL of the landing page does not change example: abcmortgage.com/ebook, it makes it fast and easy to share.
The URL is available to copy and paste from the Landing Page Builder
Commonly used for First Time Home Buyer class registration, Social Posts, ebook giveaways, and other lead generating activities.
Permalink Pages are personalized to the User with the User's information (and the company, disclosures, etc.) and can be shared across all media types.

Select Link type list.
Select Landing Page.
Using the drag and drop editor when you add a button you have the ability to link that button to a landing page.
In the Configure Landing Page link, select Landing Page button.
Select Domain from the list.
Select Save.

Clone a Permalink Landing Page
Locate the landing page in the media library.
Select to the Left.
Select Clone.
In the Clone Landing Page screen complete the following:
Enter a Name of Landing Page.
Select a Library.
This controls who can access the Landing Page by assigning a specific folder in which to house the page.

Select your company's domain name from the list.
Enter a name for the URL extension.
Example, companyname.com/permalink/housingcalculator.
Designate a Default Fallback User.
Select a user from your company to receive the form results if the link back to the sender breaks i.e., that person is no longer an active Surefire User.
Select Clone Landing Page.

Marketing
Landing Pages
Create Co-branded Permalink Landing Pages
Permalink landing pages are designed to share with unknown contacts, such as through social media or by referral partners. Alternatively, dynamic landing pages are typically shared with known contacts and are connected to their contact record in Surefire. They may contain prefilled information about the contact or their loan, and any forms completed from the dynamic landing page, such as a contact us form, will be connected to the recipient’s Surefire contact record.
One way to build referral partner relationships is to provide links to co-branded landing pages, which the referral partner can then share on social media or through email or text. This is a common request for calculators and interactives.
Clone the Layout
Select Public folder.
In the Surefire Media Library, locate the MUST BE EDITED – Permalink Cobranded Landing Page layout . Be sure you’re viewing Layouts in the top bar.
Select next to the layout.
Select Clone.
Rename the layout to include the referral partner’s name.
Save it in the LO’s folder.
Personalize the Layout.
Open the cloned layout and edit the red text with the referral partner’s information.

Marketing
Flyers
Mobile and Social Tabs in Flyers
There are three tabs Print, Mobile, Social available when editing a flyer.
The mobile version of the flyer is used if a flyer is opened from a phone or a tablet, this happens automatically based on the viewer's screen size. If there is no mobile version of the flyer set, the full-width print version is used as a single standing webpage.
The social version is a large image used in the Facebook newsfeed to entice users to click on the image and read more. If the user clicks in a section it opens to either the desktop view or the mobile view depending on the device's screen size.
The best way to see an example of this is to add one of the Surefire Created flyers and toggle through each one of the three views so you can see how they are used/set up.
Creating and using these additional views is completely optional and not required to use the flyers.
Review Add Surefire Public Flyers s for additional information.

View Flyer Activity Notifications
View Flyer Activity Notifications Surefire Flyers has its own dedicated communications channel, called Notifications, that lets users and administrators know about Flyer, Flyer Image and Flyer Signature submission and submission status updates.
When working with Flyers in Surefire, the Notifications always displayed at the top of the screen. If present, a circle with a number in it overlaid on the Notifications icon indicates how many unread notifications you have.
Select to see the list of Notifications. The screen displays:
A short list of most recent notifications
Three shortcut buttons that will take you to, respectively, Manage Signatures, Manage Images and Manger Flyers
A View All button at the bottom of the pop up that, when clicked on, takes you to the Surefire Flyers Notification page (see below).
Notifications Page
The Notifications Page, accessed via the View All button on the Notifications pop up (discussed above), displays a list of the notifications, in descending chronological order, that have been sent to you via the Surefire Flyers system.
Select an entry (i.e. row) on the Notifications Page will navigate you to the Manage [Flyer Component Type] appropriate to that Notifications (i.e.. Flyers, Images or Signatures).
Administrators and Standard Users receive different kinds of notifications:
Notifications for Standard Users
Notifications are sent to a Standard User when:
A Flyer, Signature or Flyer Image that they have submitted has been approved
A Flyer, Signature or Flyer Image that they have submitted has been rejected
A Flyer, Signature or Flyer Image that they have submitted has been edited
A Flyers Administrator has sent a message regarding one of their Flyers, Signatures or Flyer Images
Notifications for Administrators
Notifications are sent to a Administrators when a user has either edited an existing, or submitted a new Flyer, Signature or Flyer Image for approval.

Marketing
Flyers
Find and Download Flyers
A Flyer is a digitally created page or pages of responsive branded content consisting of custom formatted text blocks, icons and images that are layered on top of background images.
Once a Flyer is created in Surefire, it can be made instantly available to be employed for distribution by all other Surefire users or to just a subset thereof.
Flyers can be distributed, or shared, across multiple media channels, such as Print, PDF and Web pages, or via various social media platforms, such as Facebook, Twitter, LinkedIn and Pinterest.
Access Flyers by going to Marketing, Flyers.
Upon accessing flyers you'll be presented with a tile view of all the flyers you have access to.
The images of Flyers in a scrollable columned view that is divided into two tabs:
Private Flyers
Public Flyers
You can adjust the number of columns presented on the screen by clicking the numbers at the top right.
Icons
Hovering on the eye icon will give a large preview of the flyer.
The cloud icon will download the flyer to pdf.
The share icon will give you the various sharing options made available for that flyer. The more options, reveals: clone, edit, delete. Surefire created content displays clone only, you can clone our content then make your own edits.
When you've found the flyer you'd like to download click on the flyer.
User's signatures should automatically load onto the flyer. If you want to change the signature that appears on the flyer click the signature icon.
For Flyers that have dynamic merge fields included in their design, you can select from which User, Contact or Co-Brand Partner's Contact Record in Surefire you want data imported in order to populate those fields. Then choose the preview eye icon to see what it looks like merged in.
Finally, you can click the Load Signature button to select a Surefire user's signature to append to the Flyer.
Filter Which Flyer Thumbnail Images are Displayed On the Home/Flyers screen there are three ways to filter, i.e. limit, which Flyer Images are displayed in the scrollable column on the far right of the screen:
Search
Select Category
Public Flyers vs. Private Flyers
Search
Enter a term into the Search field near the top of the screen. This can be a key term included in the text of the Flyer or the name the Flyer was saved under in Surefire.
Select Enter.
The Flyer Thumbnail Image list will be refreshed and will include only Flyers that match your search term(s).
Select Category
When a Flyer is created in Surefire, it is assigned one or more Categories as a way to more easily organize and find Flyers within the system.
Use the Select Category drop down menu to limit the Flyer Thumbnail Image list to just those Flyers that are related to a specific topic:
Click the Select Category drop down menu, located in the upper right-hand corner of the screen.
Move your mouse pointer to the Category you want to filter the list by.
Click on that Category to select it.
The Flyer Thumbnail Image list will be refreshed and will now include only Flyers that have been assigned the Category you selected.
Public or Private Flyers
The Flyer Thumbnail Images column is divided into two tabs: Private Flyers and Public Flyers.
Public Flyers - Flyers made available to your Organization in Surefire by a Flyer administrator
Private Flyers - Flyers that you have made in Surefire and that are available for viewing/editing by you only.
Select the tab corresponding to the type of Flyers you want thumbnail images displayed for.

Marketing
Flyers
Edit a Flyer
To access the Home, Flyers, Edit screen, first select a Flyer for editing from either the Select a Flyer or the Manage Flyers screen and then select Clone.
You must have sufficient Flyer Permissions to have access to this function.
To edit from the flyers list view screen:
Edit a Flyer's Different Views Surefire Flyers are designed to be distributed, or shared, across multiple media channels (e.g. Print, PDF, Web) as well as via various social media platforms (e.g.Facebook, Twitter, LinkedIn, Pinterest), different versions of each Flyer must be created.
Flyer versions are differentiated from one another by their prescribed size, layout and resolution requirements.
On the Flyers Edit screen in Surefire, each Flyer version is displayed and edited in its own tab. These tabs are arrayed across the top of the Flyer Edit screen: Web - Web Flyers are optimized for viewing on a desktop device at 1000 x 852 pixels Mobile - Mobile Flyers are optimized for viewing on a mobile devices such as phones and tablets at 700 x 600 pixels Social Media - Social Media Flyers are optimized to use as "Hero" (profile header) images on various social media platforms at 1200 x 600 pixels
Import from PSD -
PSD-versions of Flyers are Flyers that have been created in Photoshop for import into and edit in Surefire.
Review Create a Flyer for additional information.
Edit Flyer Layers
Each component element of a Flyer (or, where applicable, Flyer page), be it the background image underlying the Flyer, selections of Text, overlaid images or indeed overlaid icons, is saved to its own Layer. A Layer can be thought of much like a transparency on which each element is placed. The amalgamation of all Layers put together is what creates the final Flyer (or Flyer page) image.
In order to edit the contents of any Layer (i.e. that component element of the Flyer), you must first select the corresponding Layer.
The Layers Pane
Layers are displayed and selected from the table in the Layers Pane.
Each row in the table corresponds to one of the Flyer's Layers
Click on a row in the table to select that Layer to use Surefire 's Flyer Editing Tools to directly edit that component element of the Flyer on the Flyer Canvas in the center of the screen.
Selected Layers will be outlined in blue on the Flyer Canvas.
The row corresponding to the currently selected Layer appears highlighted in blue.
You can resize a selected Layer by dragging-and-pulling the the corners or sides of the blue outline.
You can re-orient the angle of a selected Layer by positioning your mouse on the square that appears above the center of the blue outline (the mouse pointer will change into a cross), then clicking and holding, and then moving your mouse around to see how the Layer's orientation changes.
The left-most column of the table displays an icon that indicates whether a Layer's (i.e. row's) content consists of Text or an Image. Note that icons (described below under Flyer Editing Tools) are classified as text. Text Layers, the first words of the text included in the Layer are displayed in the table. This helps you determine which Layer is which when scrolling through the table. you can click the edit icon, displayed in the table's third column, to launch a pop up window that contains all of the text, unformatted, that's included in the Layer. You can then edit the text in this pop up as an alternative to editing it directly on the Flyer Canvas. Click Save in the pop up when you've finished making your changes. you can delete the Layer (and thereby remove the component element of your Flyer that's included on that Layer) by clicking the trash icon, located in the fourth column of the table.
Click the padlock icon to lock or unlock a layer. When a layer is locked, it cannot be moved above or below its current location in the layers order.
Flyer Edit Tools
Each component element of a Flyer, be it image or text, can be edited once the corresponding Layer has been selected.
You can select a Layer in the Layers pane alternatively, select a Layer by clicking directly on that component element of the Flyer on the Flyer Canvas in the center of the screen.
Similar to content generated using word processing software (e.g Microsoft Word), Flyer content can be edited directly on the Flyer Canvas in the center of the screen, using a combination of mouse actions such as drag-and-drop and re-sizing along with Surefire 's Flyer Editing tools.
The following Flyer Editing Tools, or functions, can be found in the Editing Icons pane, located in the upper right of the Flyers Edit screen: Add Text - Select this icon to append a Text Layer to the Flyer. Double click on the text in the Layer (The text "Add Text" appears by default) and type in whatever content you want. Use the other tools described in this section to change how the text appears. Cut, Copy and Paste - The Cut command removes selected text from its original position, while the Copy command creates a duplicate; in both cases the selected text is kept in a temporary, unseen storage tool called the clipboard. The data in the clipboard is later inserted in the position where the Paste command is issued. Bold, Italic and Underline - Select Text and then click any of these icons to add the desired type of emphasis. Line Height - Select this icon to launch a pop up that lets you specify the height, in pixels, of a text layer. Character Spacing - Select this icon to launch a screen that allows you to enter how many pixels will be inserted between text characters.
Text Alignment (Left, Center, Right and Justified) - Set text placement relative to the contours of the text Layer.
Left: The text is aligned along the left margin
Center: The text is aligned to neither the left nor right margin; there is an even gap on each side of each line.
Right: The text is aligned along the right margin
Justified: The text is aligned along the left margin, and letter- and word-spacing is adjusted so that the text falls flush with both margins Icons - Click this icon to launch a pop up containing a large selection of symbols (e.g. a paper airplane, a wrench, a check mark, a "refresh" symbol, etc).
Double click on any of these symbols to add a Layer to your Flyer containing the symbol.
Icons are considered text by the system, and thus can be edited and manipulated in the same ways text can. Font Color - Select any Text and then click this icon to launch a pop up where you specify color by either:
Selecting from a palette of 20 pre-determined colors.
Review Manage Flyer Colors for additional information.
Clicking on the Hex Color Code at the bottom of the pop up to either enter a color code directly or to launch a color selector pop up where you can select a color by appearance Undo - Click this icon to undo previous edit actions. As you regress through actions, a re-do icon is also displayed, allowing you to move backward and forward through your edits. Rotate Image - Click this button to rotate the currently selected image layer clock-wise 45-degrees. Thus, clicking this button 8 times in a row will turn your image all the way around back to the orientation it started in. Superscript and Super Subscript - Click these buttons to change the text in the currently selected text layer to either Superscript or Super Subscript. A subscript or superscript is a character (number, letter or symbol) that is (respectively) set slightly below or above the normal line of type. It is usually smaller than the rest of the text. Rotate Canvas - Click this button to change the Canvas orientation between Portrait and Landscape. Font Size - Select Text and then click this icon to launch a pop up where you specify text height in pixels. Font Selection Drop Down Menu - Select Text and then click this drop down menu to launch a pop up where you select from a list of available fonts for the text should be displayed in. Text Styles - Click this button to reveal a menu with a list of selectable Font Styles (e.g. "Heading 1" or "Modified Body") each of which reflects a set of pre-configured Font Formatting Combinations (size, color, alignment, spacing, etc).
Review Manage Flyers Fonts for additional information.
