Choose / Upload
You can add assets to your Flyer.
Select Add Custom Image.
Replace the Background Image with one chosen from the system's existing galleries of Images.
Add Flyer (i.e. replace the Flyer currently loaded onto the Edit screen with a different one)
Load a Flyer Signature.
Review Select Flyer Signature for additional information.
Add Custom Image
In the Choose / Upload section on the Flyer Edit screen, click Select Custom Image icon.
In the Select or upload an Image window displayed, you can either:
Click the Browse button to bring up your operating system's explorer selector window where you can find and select a new image to upload to the system. Note that you must click the Upload button once the selector window has closed.
Select an already-uploaded custom image by clicking on it and then clicking the Load button which then appears
Manipulate the size and orientation of the Custom Image Layer as you would any other Layer.
Replace Background Image
In the Choose/Upload pane on the right side of the Flyer Edit screen, click the Gallery icon.
In the pop up window that's displayed, click either the Custom or Public Images tab (for, respectively) images you have uploaded to Flyers or images that have been uploaded by admins for public use.
Click on the thumbnail of your desired background image.
Click the Load button in the lower right hand corner of the pop up window.
Replace the Flyer Currently Loaded onto the Edit Screen
In the Choose/Upload pane on the right side of the Flyer Edit screen, click the Flyers icon.
In the pop up window that's displayed, click either the Custom or Public Flyers tab (for, respectively) Flyers you have created or Flyers that have been created by admins for public use as templates
Click on the thumbnail of your desired Flyer.
Click the Load button in the lower right hand corner of the pop up window.
Load Flyer Signature
In the Choose/Upload pane on the right side of the Flyer Edit screen, click the Signature icon.
Click on the Signature you want included on this Flyer.
Review Select Flyer Signature for additional information.
Check a Flyer's Mobile Compatibility Surefire includes a Mobile Compatibility Check tool which provides suggestions of how you can improve your Flyer's text formatting and layout to best insure a great look and feel when your Flyer is viewed on Mobile Devices like Phones and Tablets.
To launch the Mobile Compatibility Check, click on the Mobile Phone Icon, located in the upper right hand corner of the Flyers Edit screen. A screen displays that displays formatting guidance (e.g. Font size should be between 32 and 50 pixels) with a list of which text layers said guidance should be applied to.
When you are ready to save your Flyer edits, select Save, located in the upper right hand corner of the Flyer Edit screen. This launches the Create Flyer screen, where you enter several Flyer attributes.
Review Save a Flyer for additional information.

Marketing
Flyers
Save a Flyer
From the Flyer Edit screen, once you are ready to save your changes, click the Save button, located in the upper right-hand corner of the Flyer Edit screen. This launches the Create Flyer screen, where to enter the Flyer attributes described below.
Flyers Category
When a Flyer is created in Surefire, it is assigned one or more Categories as a way to more easily organize and find Flyers within the system.
Here, you can click on the Flyers Category field to bring up a screen menu containing a list of all Flyer Categories in the system. Click the checkbox(es) next to the category or categories that you want to assign to this Flyer.
Alternatively or additionally, you can click the Add Category button (which looks like a blue square with a plus sign on it), then type a new Category name directly into the Flyers Category field and then click the Save button that now appears next to the Flyers Category heading. Title - Add or Edit the title this Flyer is saved under in Surefire.
Status
(Administrators Only) - Administrators can mark a Flyer as immediately approved upon saving. Click on the field to launch a drop-down menu that, depending on permissions, lets you select either:
Approved
Not Approved Added/Revised - Record the date this Flyer was either added to the system or revised. The system defaults to the current day's date.
You can type directly into the field (mm/dd/yyyy) or click use the interactive calendar pop-up that appears when you click on the field to select a date. Expiration Date - Enter a date on and after which this Flyer will no longer be available for use or sharing because their status will revert to unapproved.
You can type directly into the field (mm/dd/yyyy) or click use the interactive calendar pop up that appears when you click on the field to select a date.
Flyer Access
(Administrators Only) - Check one of the available options to designate access to the Flyer. Private will limit access to only the creator of the Flyer. Public will open access to all active users of the organization. Designated will open a pop-up window with a selectable organizational tree and allow for access to only be granted to specific persons/companies within an organization. Allow Co-Branding - This On/Off toggle controls the ability to be able to co-brand a flyer or not. The default setting is always set to "ON." Should it be turned "OFF," then all co-branding capabilities and tools will not be available for the flyer. Co-brand and Contact merge fields dropdowns will not show in the edit panel. Any prior existing co-brand merge fields in the flyer will be removed. And, the co-brand signature templates will not show or be available for use with the flyer. Individual Instructions and Description
The Create Flyer save pop-up includes three text fields where you can save or import formatted details associated with your Flyer. Individual Instructions - Instructions on how to use this Flyer. Especially useful for admins who would like their users to know how this Flyer is intended to be used. Description - Write a description for this Flyer. For internal use. Designed to help users remember what this Flyer is for. Content here is searchable from within other parts of the Flyers system.
For all three of these text fields, you can click on the green pencil edit icon to launch an Update Content pop-up window.
Here, in addition to most standard text formatting tools (Font type & size, Font color, Font emphasis, including strikethrough, Text alignment, Text indentation, quotation block, numbered list, bulleted list), you'll find some additional options for creating content, including:
Add/Remove Hyperlink
Add Image
Insert Table
Insert Horizontal Separator Line
Insert Symbol
Print
Edit content as HTML (convenient for when you want to paste in content created as HTML)
Social Message
Enter the Title and Metadata that will accompany this Flyer when it is shared on Social Media. Social Heading - The Bold Title that will accompany this Flyer when it is shared on Social Media Social Message - The MetaData description that will accompany this Flyer when it is shared on Social Media
Once you have entered your Flyer's attributes, select Save.

Marketing
Flyers
Share Flyer
Flyers are distributed, or shared, across multiple media channels, such as Print, PDF, and Web pages, or via various social media platforms, such as Facebook, Twitter, Google+, LinkedIn and Pinterest.
In order to share a Flyer, you must first select it from either the Select a Flyer or the Manage Flyers screen.
Review Find and Download Flyers and Manage Flyers for additional information.
Once you've selected the Flyer you want to share, scroll to the bottom of the Home / Flyers screen to the Share pane. Here you will see icons for the various share destinations (i.e. Channels and/or Platforms) that have been made available to you, per your administrator.
Select the icon(s) corresponding to the Channel or Platform you want to share the Flyer to. In each case, a different procedure, outlined below, will need to be followed.
Share to Facebook
In the Share pane, select the Facebook icon.
A new browser tab will launch and you will be taken to a Share on Facebook page.
You must provide a Facebook login and password if you have not logged in to Facebook using your current browser before.
Use the drop down menu to select how you want to share this post (for each selection except the first, you will need to specify a target value, e.g. a Facebook Friend, Group or Event):
Share On Your Timeline
Share on a Friends' Timeline
Share in a Group
Share in an Event
Share in a Private Message
Select Post to Facebook.
The Title and Description displayed at the bottom of the post cannot be edited; they were designated when the Flyer was saved.
The URL that appears under the Description at the bottom of the post cannot be changed; it is the link to the single standing webpage for your Flyer that is created and hosted by Surefire.
Share to Twitter
In the Share pane, click the Twitter icon.
A new browser tab will launch and you will be taken to a Share a link with your followers page with a URL link to the Social Media version of your Flyer along with any additional text as configured when the Flyer was saved already included. You must provide a Twitter login and password if you have not logged in to Twitter using your current browser before.
Add additional text to your tweet (optional)
Select Tweet button.
The message you see was determined when the Flyer was saved.
The URL that appears that appears in the tweet must not be changed; it is the link to the single standing webpage for your Flyer that is created and hosted by Surefire.
Share to LinkedIn
In the Share pane, select LinkedIn icon.
A new browser tab will launch and you will be taken to a Share an update page with a URL link to the Social Media version of your Flyer along with the tile and description text as determined when the Flyer was saved. You must provide a LinkedIn login and password if you have not logged in using your current browser before.
You can add an additional message in the Share and Update section (optional).
Use the Share with: drop down to choose whether you want to share your update with all LinkedIn Users or just your LinkedIn connections.
Use the Send to individuals option to send your update to individual LinkedIn connections alone with a preceding message (optional).
Select Share.
The title and description accompanying your post should not be changed; they were determined when the Flyer was saved.
The URL that appears that appears in your LinkedIn post cannot be changed. It is the link to the single standing web page for your Flyer that is created and hosted by Surefire.
Share to Pinterest
In the Share pane, click the Pinterest icon
A new browser tab will launch and you will be taken to a Pin to Pinterest page (you will have to provide a Pinterst login and password if you have not logged in to Pinterest using your current browser before).
You will be able to choose which board to pin your Flyer to. You can also create a new Pinterest board.
You should not edit the text included with the post; it was designated when the Flyer was saved.
Click the Save button.
Print your Flyer
In the Share pane, click the Print icon
A new browser tab will launch, displaying the web version of your Flyer, with the print dialogue already activated.
Confirm your printer selection and then click the Print button.
Download your Flyer to .PDF
In the Share pane, click the PDF icon
The system automatically downloads a PDF of the Web version of your Flyer to your system's default downloads store location.
Share your Flyer via direct Web Link
In the Share pane, click the Copy Link icon
A notification message will let you know that your link has been copied to your clipboard.
The next time you paste the contents of your clipboard, the contents will be the URL for the Web version of your Flyer.
You can share the link to your Flyer anywhere.

Marketing
Flyers
Select Flyer Signature
In the context of Surefire Flyers, a Signature is a block of formatted text, containing your business contact information including an identifying graphic, that is appended to the end of a Flyer.
In Surefire Flyers, you have the option to store multiple signatures and then choose which to include at the end of any given Flyer.
In order to assign a Signature to a particular Flyer, you must first select that Flyer from either the Select a Flyer or the Manage Flyers screen.
Select Signature Type
Before choosing which Signature you want to appear at the bottom of your Flyer, you must choose which type of signature you want to use.
Click on the corresponding button, located below the Canvas of a selected Flyer. Choose from either Individual or Co-Brand. Individual - Business contact info for only one individual, brand or company will appear appended to the bottom of the Flyer Co-Brand - Business contact info for two individuals, brands or companies will appear appended to the bottom of the Flyer
Load Signature
Once you have selected a Signature Type, you must select which specific Signature you want appended to your Flyer.
Select Load Signature button, located next to the Signature Type buttons described above.
A screen is generated showing thumbnail images of all the Signatures (of the type selected) that you have been granted access to.
You can filter which thumbnails are displayed for selection. Filter by:
Search
-Enter all or part of the name under which a Signature was saved to the system. Only thumbnails for Signatures corresponding to this search term will be displayed for selection. Signature Type - Use the drop down to determine whether the system displays only "Static" (i.e. Legacy, and therefore un-editable) or Dynamic (i.e. Signatures that can be edited by both the users that created them and their org's admins) thumbnails for Signatures corresponding to this search term will be displayed for selection.
Select the Signature you want to use.

Marketing
Flyers
Add and Edit a Flyer Category
When a Flyer is created in Surefire, it is assigned one or more Categories as a way to more easily organize and find Flyers within the system (for example when working with the Manage Flyers Table).
Creating and/or Deleting Categories will affect your downstream users. A created/deleted category will be added to/removed from view from any child organizations and those organizations' user accounts.
Administrators can Review, Add, Edit and Delete Flyer Categories by going to Marketing, Flyers, Manage Categories.
Review, Edit and Delete Flyer Categories
The table displayed on the Manage Flyer Categories screen displays the names of all Flyer Categories in the system. These names appear in the second, Category column of the table.
You can drag and drop categories within the table to change the priority in which they are listed. A Category's Sort Order is automatically updated after the Category is dragged and dropped.
You can sort the table by ascending or descending order by clicking on the Category column header.
For each row, i.e. Category listing, in the table, with the exception of the system category "Expired," the buttons included in the Action column allow an administrator to: Edit Category - Click the Pencil icon to launch an Edit Category pop up where you can edit the Category name. Delete Category - Click the Trash Can icon to launch a Remove Category - [Category Name] confirmation pop up.
If the Category you are trying to delete has not been assigned to any Flyers, a simple confirmation screen is displayed.
However, if the Category you are trying to delete has been assigned to any Flyers, then a screen is displayed listing all Flyers in the system that the Category you wish to Delete has been assigned to.
For each Flyer (i.e. row in the table) displayed in the pop up, click on the table cell under Category to bring up a selection pop up where you can re-assign what categories are assigned to that Flyer.
Only once you have assigned Categories to all Flyers shown in the pop up can you click on the Submit button to confirm your delete request.
Filter the Contents of the Manage Flyer Categories Table
There are two ways to filter, i.e. limit, which Flyer Categories are displayed in the Manage Flyer Categories Table: Number of Entries and Search. Number of Entries - Use the Show... entries drop down menu, located above the upper left hand corner of the table, to select how many rows should be displayed per page of the table. Select from 10, 25 or 100
Navigation buttons allowing you to move through table pages are located directly below the bottom right hand corner of the table.
Search -
Enter all or part of a Category name into the Search Field, located above the upper right-hand corner of the table, and hit Enter.
The contents of the table will be refreshed and will include only Flyer Categories that match your search term(s).
Synch Parent Categories
Click the Synch Parent Categories button to import copies of any categories that have been created for your Parent Organization that are not currently present for use in yours.
Add a Flyer Category
There are two ways to add a Flyer Category:
Add a Flyer Category from the Manager Flyer Categories Screen
Select Add Category, located in the upper right-hand corner of the screen.
An Add Category pop up is displayed. Enter a Category name and click Save.
Add a Flyer Category form the Flyer Edit , Create Flyer Screen
On the Create Flyer screen (shown whenever you save a Flyer), select Add Category button (, then type a new Category name directly into the Flyers Category field and then click the Save button that now appears next to the Flyers Category heading.

Marketing
Flyers
Branches and Organization Access to Flyers
When you add a new organization or branch to your company it is likely that you'll want the new account to start out with access to flyers. When you save a flyer you designate access to the flyer, meaning you choose who gets to access that flyer. When you create a new branch or org in your tree, that org has not had any flyer content designated to it, because it's new.
Rather than going through your flyers and saving each flyer one by one, we want to make them all (or many) available at once to the new org in the tree.
Bulk Actions
Go to the flyers list view.
Select the flyers you wish to designate or select all.
Select Bulk Actions.
Select designate access.
Select organizations you want to make the content available to.
Select Apply.

Marketing
Flyers
Create Multipage Flyers
You can create Flyers with multiple pages. A great application of the multipage Flyers function is when you want to create a presentation or sales leave-behind.
Create a Multi-Page Flyer
Go to Marketing, Flyers.
Select Create a flyer.
You must have sufficient Flyer Permissions to have access to this menu item.
From here, you can:
Build a multi-page Flyer using text and images
Assemble a multi-page Flyer out of Flyers that have already been saved in Surefire Assemble a multi-page Flyer out of individual Adobe Photoshop-generated PSD files that you upload into your multi-page Flyer one-at-a-time
Use Flyer Editor
Use the same tools and techniques outlined in Create a Flyer and Edit a Flyer s to create the first page of your Flyer. Then select Add New Page button.
A new blank canvas page is added along with page navigation buttons.
You can populate the content of this page of your multi-page Flyer using the tools and techniques outlined in Create a Flyer and Edit a Flyer.
Alternatively, you can populate the content of this page by adding a Flyer that was already created in Surefire, or by importing an Adobe Photoshop-generated PSD file. Both of these methods are covered below.
Using Existing Flyers
From the Create Open / Multipage Canvas tab under
Marketing > Flyers > Create a flyer, select the Flyers icon in the Create/Upload panel.
A selection pop-up window is displayed from which you can select the existing Flyer(s) you want to include in your new multi-page Flyer.
On this pop-up, you can toggle back and forth between tabs containing Custom Flyers that you have created yourself and Public Flyers that have been created for and shared to your organization.
Once you have selected a first previously-created Flyer to include, click the Add New Page button (as described above) to add an additional blank canvas to your multi-page Flyer. Then, if you wish, you can once again click the Flyers icon in the Create/Upload panel and repeat the steps as outlined above in order to select another previously-created Flyer for inclusion in your new multi-page Flyer.
Using PSDs Files
Go to Marketing, Flyers, Create a flyer and click on the Import from PSD button.
Review and complete the instructions Import from PSD , in Edit a Flyer
Once you have selected a first previously-created PSD to include, click the Add New Page button (as described above) to add an additional blank canvas to your multi-page Flyer. Then once again click the Import from PSD button and repeat the steps as outlined above in order to select another previously-created PSD for inclusion in your new multi-page Flyer.
Download a Multi-Page Flyer as a PDF Currently, multi-page Flyers are only distributed via exporting them as a PDF.
Note that before a Flyer can be downloaded as a PDF and therefore distributed, a signature must be included on at least on of its pages in order for the Flyer to be in compliance.
Once a multi-page Flyer has been saved, it can be selected by users from either the Select a Flyer or the Manage Flyers screen.
Once you've selected the multi-page Flyer you want to export as a PDF, scroll to the bottom of the Home / Flyers screen to the Share pane. Here you will see an icon for Sharing to PDF.
Click the Share to PDF icon and the system will automatically download a PDF of the Web version of your multi-page Flyer to your system's default downloads store location.

Marketing
Flyers
Edit Default Company Flyer Signature
In the context of Surefire Flyers, a Signature is a re-usable area of formatted text, containing business contact information as well as perhaps an identifying graphic, that is usually appended to the bottom of a Flyer.
Default Signatures
All Surefire Flyers users have access to a Default Signature that may include custom contact information that's been copied from the user's own Surefire User account or Contact Record.
A Default Signature is created for the user the first time that a Surefire User logs in to Flyers using the company template.
Signature Structures
Default Signatures are based on a Signature Template, or "Structure," that is created by a Surefire Flyers Administrator. The Signature Structure is where the Default Signature's appearance attributes such as fonts, colors and/or included graphics are determined. It can also include dynamic text and image fields (e.g. [Name], [Contact Number], or [Contact Image]) into which content is merged from a Surefire Flyers user's Surefire account the first time that they log in to Flyers.
Create Default Company Signature
To create your company’s default signature.
Select Settings.
Select Signature Structure.
The signature canvas you are provided is approximately ⅓ of a letter size flyer. If your company flyers need more room, and less signature space, don’t worry you can adjust the placement of the objects on the canvas by clicking on them and arranging them how you like.
You can place the objects either at the top, bottom or middle of the signature canvas it is completely up to you.
The background of the signature canvas is clear so it will not disturb your flyer content when laid onto your flyer.
To add merge fields to the signature select User Merge fields drop down.
Select inside the text-box and select the merge field from list.
Set Up The Co-Brand Signature Default
You will notice you have co-brand signatures as well. To set up the default co-brand signature click co-brand.
Go to Flyers, Settings.
Select Signature Structure, Co-Brand.
To use co-brand merge fields in the signature use the Co-Brand Merge Fields drop down. Click inside the text-box and then click the drop-down menu to select the desired merge field.
Mobile Signature
You will also notice the tab Mobile Signature next to print. Each Surefire Flyer automatically converts itself to a single standing webpage, so you can share the flyer using a link, instead of the old fashioned way.
Surefire Flyers use the latest technology and automatically detect if the reader of the flyer is looking at it on their phone, if so, the flyer re-sizes itself accordingly.
To set up a mobile signature, click mobile and use the editing tools to arrange the items on the mobile signature canvas to suit your needs.
Manage Signatures
In addition to the Default Signature, Surefire Users with sufficient permissions can create, edit and delete alternate Signatures.
Some teams need special team signatures, or some users may want special logos or emblems added to their signatures, for those who have considerations beyond the default signature a user can add their own signature and customize it.
The user's custom signature must be approved by an admin before they can use it.
Review and manage signatures by going to Marketing, Flyers, Signatures. You must have sufficient Flyer Permissions to have access to this menu item.
To view flyers created by other people in your organization click on my org (if they are directly in your same branch) or click on child org, if they are downstream.
From this view, you may preview the signature, edit it, reject it or delete it.
Add a Flyer Signature
Users with sufficient permissions can create custom Signatures that will be available, as an alternative to their Default Signature, for inclusion at the end of any of their Flyers.
Go to Marketing, Flyers.
Select Manage Signatures.
Select Add Signature.
The Edit Signatures screen is displayed, pre-populated with the admin-created design for your Default Signatures (i.e. Individual and Co-brand in both Web and Mobile versions).
Customize your Signature:
Toggle On/Off the Guidelines Grid - If desired, you can use the Guidelines Grid to ensure that the various elements of your Signature are in line with one another.
Select Individual or Co-brand Signature - select the appropriate button to select whether this Signature will include one or two business Contacts.
Add or Edit Text Using the Editing Tools
Review Edit a Flyer for additional information.
Upload Image(s)
Review Add a Custom Image for additional information
Select toggle for: Mobile version - appears when your Flyer is viewed online from a mobile device Web - The Web (full width) version will appear on printed and web viewed Flyers
Select Preview to see the signature.
Select Save Signature.
Enter a name for this signature.
Select OK.
If you have Edit access without admin approval, your custom Flyer signature will be available for use immediately.
If you have Edit access with admin approval, a notification will be sent to your Surefire Flyers admin(s) who will then approve, edit or reject your custom Flyer signature.
Edit a Flyer Signature
You can edit any Custom Flyer Signatures you have created and/or have access to.
Go to Marketing, Flyers.
Select Manage Signatures.
Use any combination of Sorting, Filtering or Searching the table to locate the Signature you want to edit: Choose Own or Others Signatures - If you have sufficient Flyer Permissions, you have the option to view and therefore edit signatures authored by other users. To view these signatures, toggle the My Org's Signature and/or the My Child Org's Signature buttons.
Toggle the My Signature button to view only Signatures that you have authored.
Filter which Signature Types to display - Click on the Signature Type drop-down menu, located above upper right-hand corner of the table, to reveal a dropdown. Approved Signatures - Signatures that have been approved by an administrator so that they can be shared Unapproved Signatures - Signatures that have been submitted but not yet approved by an administrator for use Rejected Signatures - Signatures that have been submitted but rejected by an administrator for use Deleted Signatures - Signatures created in Surefire that have been deleted
Enter a term into the Search field, located above the upper right-hand corner of the table. This term can be all or part of:
The Signature's Title
This Signature's Author's name
The Contact associated with the signature
The Signature type (Cobrand or Individual)
Any term that appears in any other column of the table
The contents of the table are refreshed and will include only Signatures with attributes that match your search term(s).

Manage Flyers
You can view an interactive, sortable, filter-able table of all Flyers saved in the system that your user account has access to by going to Flyers and click the list view.
The table displayed on this screen, in addition to displaying your Surefire Flyers' vital statistics like Title, Thumbnail image, Author, Type, Creation Date & Organizational Unit to which the Flyer has been designated available (i.e. visible and usable), is also where administrators review the status of user-authored Flyers that have been submitted for approval so that they can be used and shared.
Furthermore, it is from this table that the following Flyer Actions can be taken:
View/Edit
Delete
Approve/unapprove
Reject (Administrators Only)

Filter by Organization,
Filter by Flyer Type
Designate Number of Flyers shown

(Available to Administrators Only)

Organizational Unit
Organizational Unit's Parent Org
Organizational Unit's child org(s).

Sync Surefire Authored Flyers
(Available to Administrators Only)
The Surefire Team is always generating new Flyer content to share with Surefire users.
Click the Sync Surefire Flyers button to retrieve the latest flyers created by the Surefire for users to edit and make their own.
Purge Deleted Flyers
(Available to Administrators Only)
Click the Purge button to permanently remove Flyers that have been deleted by users.
Bulk Delete
To delete to more than one flyer at once click the checkboxes next to each entry in the table that you'd like to remove. Then click bulk actions, then click delete.
Category Type
Click on the Category Type drop-down menu, located above the center of the table, to reveal a drop-down menu to select any combination of selections of Flyer Categories to display , click the Select All checkbox to select all:
Flyer Type
Click on the Flyer Type drop-down menu, located in the upper right-hand corner of the table, to reveal a dropdown where you can toggle on and off any combination of the following selections (click the "Select All" checkbox to select all):
Select all - Select all checkboxes for the below described Flyer types. This will result in all Flyer types being displayed in the table. Custom Flyers - Flyers that have been created by Flyers users Public Flyers - Flyers that have been created by an administrator and made available to all Surefire users Approved Flyers - User-submitted Flyers that have been approved by an administrator so that they can be shared Unapproved Flyers - User-authored Flyers that have been submitted for approval, but for which no action has yet been taken by an administrator Rejected Flyers - User-submitted Flyers that have been rejected by an administrator so that they are not available to be used and/or shared Deleted Flyers - Flyers created in Surefire that have been deleted Expired Flyers - Flyers who have achieved their Expiration Date and are therefore set to unapproved status.
Search
Enter a term into the Search Field, located just below the Flyer Type drop down menu described above. This can be all or part of:
The Title of a Flyer
A key term included in the Title of a Flyer
A key term included in the body of a Flyer
Enter - the contents of the table will be refreshed and will include only Flyers with attributes that include your search term(s).
Columns in the Manage Flyers Table
You can sort the table by column in ascending or descending order by clicking on any of these column headings once or twice respectively. Title - Displays the Flyer's title as well as any categories associated with it Image - Displays a thumbnail image of the Flyer. When you click on this thumbnail, a horizontally scrollable pop up overlay is displayed which allows you to scroll through a preview of each of the Flyer's versions (Web, Mobile and Social) Created By - Shows the name of the Surefire User who created the Flyer Created Date - Shows the date the Flyer was created Designated Orgs - Shows the name of the Organizational Unit(s) to which the Flyer is visible and available for use Created Orgs
-Shows the name of the Organizational Unit(s) by which the Flyer was created Status - Shows if the Flyer has been approved by an administrator for sharing or not Type - Shows if the Flyer is Public (Flyers that have been created by an administrator and made available to all Surefire users) or Custom (Flyers that have been created by Surefire Users)
Action
-For each row, i.e. Flyer listing, in the table, all Flyer Action buttons are included in this column. See below for details.
Flyer Actions
For each row, i.e. Flyer listing, in the table, the buttons included in the Action column correspond to the following functions: Edit - Clicking the pencil icon takes you to the Edit the Flyer screen.
For administrators, this button is convenient when a user has created a Flyer that only needs minor changes; The administrator can make the edits and then approve the Flyer. View - When you clicking this "eye" icon, a horizontally scrollable pop up overlay is displayed which allows you to see each of the Flyer's views (Web, Mobile and Social) Delete - Deletes the Flyer. You can always view deleted Flyers (see "Flyer Type" above) and, should you wish, retrieve them.
Approve
(Available to Administrators Only) - When and administrator Approves a Flyer, a notification is sent to the user that their Flyer has been approved and is now available to be shared.
Reject
(Available to Administrators Only)- When and administrator Rejects a Flyer, a notification is sent to the user that their Flyer has been rejected, and is not available to be shared. Clone - Creates a copy of the Flyer which is opened for Editing and Saving under a new name.

Marketing
Flyers
Manage Flyer Permissions
There are several ways an administrator can manage how freely Flyer Users can edit, submit, manage and use Flyers and Flyer Components (such as images, signatures and fonts) as well as to which Channels they can share Flyers.
Administrators can set Global Permissions (that apply to all Users) and, simultaneously, set permission levels on a user-by-user basis. User-specific permissions trump Global Permissions.
Manage Global Permissions for Flyers
Global Permissions determine the actions and features which all users will have access to use when in Flyers.
Administrators manage Global Permissions by going to Flyers > Settings and then clicking on the Global Permissions tab.
Permissions granted on this page are applied to all users by default. Managing Flyer Permissions for Individual users is also possible.
Global Distribution Permissions
In this section of the page, Administrators choose which channels Flyer users will have the option to share the Flyers across by selecting or de-selecting any combination of the checkboxes next to: Facebook - Allows for sharing to Facebook Twitter - Allows for sharing to Twitter LinkedIn - Allows for sharing to LinkedIn Pinterest - Allows for sharing to Pinterest PNG - Downloads a Flyer as a PNG File (an image format commonly used for social images) Generate Link - Generates a web link used to embed a Flyer on websites and in emails PDF - Downloads a Flyer as a PDF file (to prevent edits) Get Download Link - Generates a download link. Then, when used and the download link is clicked, downloads as a PDF file JPEG - Downloads a Flyer as a JPEG file Get JPEG Download Link - Generates a download link. Then, when used and the download link is clicked, downloads as a JPEG file. This format is best used with Instagram sharing.
Editing Permissions
Administrators use the checkboxes to assign all users one of the following levels of Flyer editing permissions:
Edit access with admin approval
Regular Users in your organization can make changes to Flyers, text templates and signatures, however these changes are contingent upon Administrator approval. That is, when users save their changes, those changes cannot be immediately included in any shared or distributed Flyers, but rather are submitted to an administrator for review and approval or rejection.
Edit access without admin approval
When Regular Users save changes to Flyers, text templates and signatures, these changes are immediately applied and can be included in any shared or distributed Flyers.
By giving this right, you are allowing Regular Users to act as a Flyers admin for your organization.
Read & Share Only
Gives Regular Users the ability to use administrator-approved signatures and templates and use & share administrator-approved Flyers.
Manage Individual User Flyer Permissions
As mentioned above, Administrators can grant permissions to access Flyer actions and features on a user-by-user basis.
Manage Individual User Flyer Permissions under
Flyers, Manage Users.
A table listing all Flyer users becomes available, users are added to the table upon logging into Flyers for the first time.
You can edit a user's individual Flyer Permissions by clicking in the Actions column for the user's row in the table. This takes you to the Edit User screen.
Edit User Screen
User Contact Details
Edit a user's First and Last name as it appears in the system as well as their email address
Distribution Permissions
Choose which channels this user will have the option to share Flyers across by selecting or de-selecting any combination of the check boxes.
Editing Permissions
Assign this users one of the available levels of Flyer editing permissions.

Marketing
Flyers
Manage Flyer Signature Structure
All Surefire Flyers users have access to a Default Signature that is based on an Administrator-designed Signature Template.
A Signature Structure allows administrators to ensure that Flyer Signatures remain on-brand throughout their organization. This is because the Signature Structure is where default Signature appearance attributes such as fonts, colors, and/or included graphics are determined.
Edit Your Flyer Signature Structure
Administrators can edit their organization's Signature Structure to determine the format of every user's Default Flyer's Signature.
Changes made to an organization's Flyer Signature Structure are, upon saving, automatically propagated throughout the system so that users will see these changes in the default Signature that gets displayed as the default, base signature whenever they go to Add a Flyer Signature.
Review Edit Default Company Flyer Signature for additional information.
To Edit your organization's Flyer Signature Structure:
Go to Marketing, Flyers.
Select Settings.
Click Signature Structure.
The Edit Signatures Structure screen displays. If this is the first time you're editing your organization's Signature Structure, you will see the Surefire authored default Signature Structure displayed.
Customize your Signature Structure:
Toggle On/Off the Guidelines Grid
If desired, you can use the Guidelines Grid to ensure that the various elements of your Signature are in line with one another.
Toggle between the Individual or Co-brand Signature Structure
Click on the appropriate button to select whether you are editing the Signature Structure for the Default Signature that will include one or two business Contacts.
Toggle between Web and Mobile Versions
Every Signature in Surefire Flyers consists of two versions to accommodate the formatting differences inherent to the Web and Mobile versions of Flyers.
The Web (full width) version will appear on printed and web viewed Flyers; the mobile version will appear when your Flyer is viewed online from a mobile device.
Toggle between Web and Mobile to ensure that the appearance of both versions of your Signature Structure is satisfactory.
Adjust Size and Placement of the Profile Image and Organization Logo
The profile image, which shows a user’s picture, and the Organization Logo are both imported from a Flyer User's Surefire account the first time that they log in to Flyers.
You can resize either of these image templates by dragging-and-pulling the corners or sides of the blue outline.
You can also move either image template around within the Signature layout by dragging and dropping.
Adjust the Vertical Dividing Bar
You can re-size, move, or even delete the vertical divider.
Select Merge Fields
Merge fields are used to populate the user’s information onto their Signature.
Click on Select Fields to launch a drop-down menu where you can choose which Merge Fields are included in the default text box.
If a selection is greyed out, it means that it is already in use on this Signature Structure.
Add or Edit Text Using the Editing Tools - Use any of the Editing Tools to format the contents of your Signature Structure.
Review Edit a Flyer for additional information.
Upload Image(s) -
Review Edit a Flyer for additional information. Reset your Signature Structure - Click the Reset button at any time to revert the design of the Signature Structure to the Surefire authored default Signature Structure Preview Your Flyer Signature Structure - select preview view button to see a pop-up window showing what your Signature Structure will look like.
Select Save Signature Structure.
A confirmation notification appears once the system succeeds in updating your Signature Structure.

Marketing
Flyers
Manage Flyers Fonts
You have the option to select from a list of Fonts available for use in your Flyers. This list is found within the Font Selection Drop Down Menu.
This list of available fonts is managed by going to Flyers, Settings, Fonts tab. You must have sufficient Flyer Permissions to have access to this menu item.
The screen has two sections: Manage Styles - Create and manage Font Formatting Combination Shortcuts (e.g. Font, Font size, Font color etc) that you can then quickly access and apply to your various Flyers. Manage Fonts - Import, Delete or Deactivate which Fonts will be available for use in your organization's Flyers.
Manage Font Styles
A Font Style is a combination of Font Formatting selections that have been saved under a single name (e.g. "Heading 2" or "Modified Body") so that they can be quickly and consistently applied throughout one or more Flyers.
Add a Font Style:
Select Add Styles.
The Add/Edit Style pop up is displayed.
Enter a Style Name for your new Font Style (Heading 1).
This is the name that will appear in the Text Styles drop down menu when it's accessed from the Edit Flyer screen.
Use the various menus to assign formatting to your Font Style. Font Color - Specify the color of this Font Style by either:
Selecting from a palette of 20 pre-determined colors (Read More)
Clicking on the Hex Color Code at the bottom of the pop up to either enter a color code directly or to launch a color selector pop up where you can select a color by appearance Bold, Italic and Underline - Apply the desired type of emphasis to your Font Style Superscript and Super Subscript - Select applicable options to change the text for this Font Style to either Superscript or Super Subscript.
A subscript or superscript is a character (number, letter or symbol) that is (respectively) set slightly below or above the normal line of type. It is usually smaller than the rest of the text. Letter Spacing - Enter how many pixels will be inserted between text characters Font Size - Specify text height in pixels Font - Select the actual font from the list of Fonts that have been loaded into Surefire Flyers.
Review the preview of the Font Style in the Sample Text panel.
Select Save.
Edit and Delete Font Styles
Locate the Font Style you want to Edit or Delete by doing any combination of the following:
Enter all or part of the Font Style name into the Search field.
Sort the table of Font Styles by attribute in ascending or descending order by clicking on the associated column header (e.g. Created by).
Scroll through the pages of the table using the navigation buttons in the lower right (Previous, [Page Number], Next).
For the Font Style select either Edit or Delete, in the Action column.
Edit - complete the edit as applicable
Delete - select OK in the confirmation screen
Manage Fonts Table
The Manage Font section displays the names of all Fonts that have been loaded into the Surefire Flyers system for available use in Flyers. Title - the Font names and rendered in the table in their actual font. Created By - displays whom the Font was uploaded by. Created Date - when the Font was created For each row, i.e. Font listing, in the table, the buttons included in the Action column allow an administrator to: Delete Font - icon to launch a Delete Font confirmation screen, select OK to confirm the delete request.
Action - Activate or Deactivate the font using the slide selector to show or hide, the font as an available selection when editing Flyers.
Filter the Contents of the Manage Fonts Table
There are two ways to filter, i.e. limit, which Fonts are displayed in the Manage Fonts Table: Number of Entrie s - Use the Show... entries drop down menu, located above the upper left hand corner of the table, to select how many rows should be displayed per page of the table. Select from 10, 25, 50 or 100. Navigation buttons allowing you to move through table pages are located directly below the bottom right hand corner of the table. Search - Enter all or part of a Font name into the Search Field, select Enter. The contents of the table is refreshed and includes only Fonts that match your search term(s).
Add a Font
Administrators can upload new Fonts to the system that are available for use in the creation and editing of Flyers.
Select Add Font.
Add/Edit Font screen displays
In the Please select a font filed select an option from the list.
Select Save.
Font Options
We understand that maintaining your brand standards is very important to you.
Surefire Flyer uses the Google font library. If you use a font that is not found in the library use google to find the substitute. For example, you could Google, times new roman google font substitute, and you will find a suitable font.

Manage Flyer Images
You can view an interactive, sortable, filter-able table of all Flyer Background Images saved in the system. You must have sufficient Flyer Permissions to have access to this menu item. Go to Marketing, Flyers, Manage Images.
The table displayed on the Manage Images screen, in addition to displaying your Surefire Flyer Background Images' vital statistics like Title, an Image Thumbnail, Author, Creation Date, Image Type (see below for details) & the Organizational Unit for whom this image's use has been authorized by admins, is also where you review the status of user-created Flyer Background Images that have been submitted for approval so that they can be made available to other Surefire users in your organization.
Additionally, multiple Flyer Background Image Actions can be taken.
Delete - this function is only available to Administrators
Approve
Reject
Message
Filter the Contents of the Manage Flyer Background Images Table
There are five ways to filter, i.e. limit, which Flyer Background Images are displayed in the Manage Flyer Images Table: Organization, Purge, Image Type, Number of Entries and Search. Organization - Available to Administrators only
You can choose whether to display only Flyer Background Images made available to to the currently selected Organizational Unit or, alternatively, to display all Flyer Background Images saved in Surefire.
To make your selection, click on the corresponding button located above the table in the center of the screen. Select:
[Current Organizational Unit Name]
Parent/Child Org's
Purge
The Purge button, located above the table in the center of the screen, is used to permanently remove images whose status is deleted.
To Purge deleted images:
Select Purge.
The table is filtered to show only images whose statuses are set to deleted.
Select the check box for any row that corresponds to a status: deleted image you want to permanently remove from the system.
Click Purge Selected.
Image Type
Click on the Image Type drop down menu, located above upper right-hand corner of the table, to reveal a list where you can toggle on and off any combination of the following selections. You can also check
Select All: Custom Images - Flyer Background Images that have been uploaded by a Surefire user Public Images - Flyer Background Images that have been created by an administrator and made available to all Surefire users Approved Images - User-submitted Flyer Background Images that have been approved by an administrator and are therefore available for use by all Surefire Flyers users Unapproved Images - User-created Flyer Background Images that have been submitted for approval, but for which no action has yet been taken by an administrator Rejected Images - User-created Flyer Background Images that have been rejected by an administrator so that they are not available for use by all Surefire Flyers users Deleted Images - Flyer Background Images uploaded to Surefire that have been deleted
Number of Entries
Use the Show... entries list, located above the upper left-hand corner of the table, to select how many rows should be displayed per page of the table. Select from:
10
25
50
100
Navigation buttons allowing you to move through table pages are located directly below the bottom right-hand corner of the table.
Search
Enter a term into the Search Field, located just below the Flyer Type drop down menu described above. This can be all or part of: a key term included in the Title of the Image any term that appears in any other column of the table i.e. Image author's name, Creation Date, Creation Org, Status or Image Type. Enter - The contents of the table are refreshed and will include only Flyer Background Images with attributes that match your search term(s).
Columns included in the Manage Flyer Background Images Table
There are eight columns in the Manage Flyer Background Images Table.
You can sort the table by column in ascending or descending order by clicking on that column heading once or twice respectively. Title - Displays the name a Flyer Background Image was saved under. Image - Displays a thumbnail of the Flyer Background Image. When you click on this thumbnail, a horizontally scrollable pop-up overlay is displayed which allows you to scroll through each of the Images views (Web, Mobile and Social) Created By - Shows the name of the Surefire User who created the Flyer Background Image
Created Date
-Shows the date the Flyer Background Image was created Designated Orgs - If an admin has specified only a limited subset of your company's Org Units (i.e. Child Companies) for whom this image's use has been authorized, a View Orgs button will appear in this column. When clicked, this button brings up an org selection pop up. Created Orgs - Shows the name of the Organizational Unit under which the Flyer Background Image was created Status - Shows if the Flyer background Image has been approved by an administrator for use or not Type - Shows if the Flyer Background Image is a Public (Images that have been created by an administrator and made available to all Surefire users) or Custom (Public Flyers that have been cloned and then modified). You can click on the entry in this column to toggle back and forth (between Custom and Public) Action - For each row, i.e. Flyer Background Image, in the table, all Action buttons are included in this column.
Flyer Background Image Actions
For each row, i.e. FlyerBackground Image, in the table, the buttons included in the Action column allow an administrator to: Delete - Deletes the Flyer Background Image. Note that you can always view deleted Images (see "Image Type" above) and, should you wish, retrieve them. Approve - Approve a Flyer Background Image, a notification is sent to the user that their Image has been approved and is now available for use. Reject - Reject a Flyer Background Image, a notification is sent to the user that their Image has been rejected, and is not made available for use. Message - Allows you to send a message to the creator of the Flyer Background Image which is received as a notification. This function is convenient when you need the creator to make a change to their Image, but do not want to open a new, separate communication thread (such as an email).

Once you create or locate the Collection you want to deploy in the Media Library go to Marketing, Media Library select the Create Deployment to launch the Deployment Wizard. From there you'll start the process of setting up your One Time or Recurring Deployment from your collection.
If you are creating a new collection, the Create Deployment button appears after the collection is Saved.
Alternatively you can navigate to Marketing, Deployment Center to access the Deployment Center, the hub of all your outbound marketing efforts in Surefire. From here, you can schedule and deploy any digital media accessible to you in your Media Library, including media created by yourself, your Company, or Surefire.
On the Deployment Center page you can see the status and results of your marketing activities.
You can select Create Deployment from any tab to begin the process of deploying content.
The summary tabs only include marketing initiated from the Deployment Center; they do not currently include any media sent out via Workflows or Rules.
Scheduled
Tab
Shows you a table of any One-Time or Recurring Deployments that are schedule, either by you or an Administrator, to go out to your database on your behalf.
The table is organized as follows: Deployment - Name of the Deployment that links out to configuration details along with the option to Cancel the Deployment Scheduled - Date/time of deployment displayed in the Company Time Zone User - Name of user that deployed the deployment Collection - Name of Content Collection being sent
Media Type -
Included Content Collection Media Type Recurring - Whether Deployment is One-time (No) or Recurring (Yes)
Audience Size -
Total number of Contacts being Deployed to If you have multiple media types in the same Content Collection scheduled to be deployed, they will each have their own line item in the Scheduled Table.
You can perform the following actions from the Scheduled tab: Cancel Deployment - Click on the Deployment Name to bring up Deployment Details window which has a button to Cancel Deployment Filter - Filter table by Deployment Type (One-Time, Recurring) and/or Media Type (Email, Text Messages, Social) Add/Remove Columns - Click Columns to add/remove any column other than Deployment Search - Type in the search box to find any Deployments by name
Deployed
This tab contains a summary of all Past Deployment details.
Review View Past Deployments for additional information.
Available Subscriptions
This tab displays all Recurring Deployments created by you or by an administrator on behalf of your Company.
The table is organized as follows: Deployment - Name of the Deployment that links out to View Recurring Deployment Details Level - If the deployment Level listed reflects your company name, it indicates it was created by an Administrator for use by the entire Company. Myself, indicates the deployment was created only for you. Created - Date/Time of when the Recurring Deployment was created Next Deployment - Upcoming Date/Time of next scheduled Recurring Deployment Subscribed - If you are Subscribed you will see a checkmark. If you are not Subscribed, you will see a plus sign.
You can perform the following actions from the Campaigns tab: View Recurring Deployment Details - Click on the Deployment Name to bring up the Recurring Deployment Details window. Subscribe/Unsubscribe - Click the Subscribe button to Subscribe to a Deployment. Alternately, for Deployments, you are subscribed to already, hover over and click the Subscribe button to Unsubscribe.
You are automatically subscribed to any Deployments at the Level of Myself and cannot change their Subscription Status. Search - Type in the search box to find any Deployments by name
My Subscriptions
This tab summarizes the Recurring Deployments to which you have Subscribed. The table contains similar information and actions as in the Recurring tab with the exception of the following: Pause/Resume Button - For Active Subscriptions, you can Pause. This stops any Recurring Deployments from going out. When Paused, you have the option to Resume. Status Column - Indicates if a Subscription is Active or Paused.
Review Subscribe to a Recurring Deployment for additional information.
Canceled
Any Scheduled Deployments that were Canceled will appear in this tab. The table contains similar information and actions as the Scheduled tab with the exception of a column for the Date/Time of Cancellation.
Errors
If a deployment did not reach a contact, this is the first place to check to see if an error kept your deployment from reaching the appropriate contact.
Any Scheduled Deployment that experienced Errors appear in this tab. The table includes the deployment name, time at which the deployment event encountered an error, contact to whom the deployment was addressed, the Media Collection, and the Media Type.

Deployment Center
Create a Deployment
Deployments are considered email blasts or email broadcasts. You can send Emails, Texts, and Social marketing materials from your Media Library directly to your database by Creating Deployments.
Go to Marketing, Media Library.
Open/Edit the Email, Text, or Social collection you want to deploy.
Select Create Deployment.
If you are creating a new collection, the Create Deployment button appears after the collection is Saved.
Alternatively, Navigate to Marketing, Deployment Center, click the Create Deployment button to start the process.
Select either: One-Time Deployment, a one-off deployment that only happens once. It is most commonly used or Recurring Deployment is scheduled to be deployed on a daily / weekly / monthly / yearly basis
The Deployment Workflow guides you through the process. You can navigate through the steps using the Previous and Next buttons. If you exit the Deployment workflow at any point, the next time you click Create Deployment you'll be asked if you want to Continue Where You Left Off or Start Fresh.

Create a Recurring Deployment
A Recurring Deployment is a Content Collection that you want to schedule and send to your Contacts on an ongoing and consistent basis.
This content could be anything from a weekly email newsletter to a Happy Halloween text message. Setting up a Recurring Deployment is similar to the steps for a One-Time Deployment with a few additional details.
The Deployment workflow guides you through the following steps:
General
Select Content Collection
Audience Builder
Confirm & Send
You can navigate through the steps using the Previous and Next buttons. If you exit the Deployment workflow at any point, the next time you click Create Deployment you'll be asked if you want to Continue Where You Left Off or Start Fresh.
General
Enter a Deployment Name.
In the Who is this deployment for? field select: For Myself - sends an email to your Contacts on your own behalf. For my Company - Allows others to subscribe to your Recurring Deployment. Only available if you are an Admin, allows you to send to other Users' Contacts while still having the email appear to come from the User who owns the Contact.
A standard user's ability to deploy on Behalf of Your Company can be granted or restricted with the Org User Deployment permission located in Roles/Permissions. If permission is not granted, this deployment option will not appear.
In the How often do you want this deployment to occur? field select an option from the list. This screen is dynamic, and the options are based on your selection.
Weekly
Choose the day or days of the week you want your Content to Deploy on. If you want it to go out every weekday, you will select all of the weekdays from the dropdown.
Weekly setting also acts as a Daily setting, as you can select only a particular day.
Optional you can
Select All Days or Remove All Days.
Monthly
In the Choose Months field select the months you want the Deployment to go out on.
You can
Select All Months for a true monthly newsletter, or you can pick just a few months out of the year, for instance, if you want to email out a Quarterly Report.
In Select what day of the month to send select:
Exact Day of Month
-choose the exact date you want to Deploy. To accommodate all months, options range from 1-27. Specific Day of the Week - choose which week you want to Deploy ranging from 1st to 4th. You can choose more than one week. Select which day of that week you want to Deploy.
Yearly
Use this setting for a Deployment that you want to go out on an annual basis, such as a holiday-themed Content Collection.
Enter the day and month of the year that you want the deployment to generate.
Time of Day
Enter the Time of Day to Start Deployment. Select the hour and minute (in 5-minute intervals) as well as AM/PM.
The Time Zone is always set to your Company Time Zone.
This field is required for all recurring deployments.

Choose a collection.

For my Company.

Deployment Center
Subscribe to a Recurring Deployment
Recurring Deployments are unique in that they require a user to subscribe to the deployment in order for it to go out on their behalf.
The creating user is automatically subscribed for any Recurring Deployments created For Myself. However, for Recurring Deployments created For the Company, users must Subscribe to the Deployment from the Available Subscriptions section of the Deployment Center, even the creating user.
Subscribe to a Recurring Deployment
Go to Marketing, Deployment Center.
Select Available Subscriptions.
Select the Subscribe button for the deployment you want to send.
Build Your Audience for each Media Type.
Select Save Audience in each Media Type.
When you have selected and Built an Audience for each Media Type you want to include, return to Audience Builder Overview tab.
Select Save Audience & Subscribe.
Unsubscribe from a Recurring Deployment
To Unsubscribe from a Company Recurring Deployment:
Go to either the Available Subscriptions or the My Subscriptions tab.
Hover on Subscribed.
The system changes the display to now appear as a button reading Unsubscribe.
Click Unsubscribe.
Select Yes I am sure! to confirm the UnSubscription.

Deploy Content for Your Company
As an admin you can configure deployments that are available for users in your company to subscribe to, including One-Time Deployments.
Select either One-Time Deployment or Recurring Deployment. This example uses One Time Deployment.
In the Who is this deployment for? section select either
For Myself
For My Company
If this is for a Recurring Deployment, choosing For My Company makes the Deployment available to users of your company to subscribe to.
For a One-Time Deployment, selecting this option engages Open Deployment Company Configuration.
This four-step workflow provides choices for your Users and Companies you wish to Deploy on behalf of.
Companies
Complete the following fields:
Select Companies - choose which Companies in your Hierarchy you wasnt to include for your deployment
Include Child Companies? - select Yes to include all of the Child Companies beneath the higher level Companies you choose. In a situation where you have three first-tier Companies each with 10 Companies underneath them, choosing this option means you don't have to individually select all 30 Companies to include them.
Who Will the Deployment come From? - defaults to the Individual User. In this scenario, each email to a Contact comes from the email address of the User who Owns the Contact.
I want to include all current and future users of selected companies. - select Yes will include all current and future Users within selected Companies.
If set to Yes, you will effectively skip
Include Users.
Select Next.
Users Inclusions
If you selected No in I want to include all current and future users of selected companies in the previous screen, you must manually select Users from the dropdown that you wish to be part of this Deployment.
In the Select Users to Include field locate the users you want to add. You can use the list to filter by:
Users by Company, with Users in My Organization showing up first.
If you have selected other Companies, you will see the Company Name listed below the User.
As you add users, the Company Name appears in the summary table of included users.
Select Include User.
Add additional users as needed.
Select Next.
Exclude Users
If you selected to Include All Users previously, in this step you can exclude specific Users from your Deployment.
In the Select Users to Exclude field locate the users you want to remove. You can use the list to filter by:
Users by Company, with Users in My Organization showing up first.
If you have selected other Companies, you will see the Company Name listed below the User.
As you exclude users, the Company Name appears in the summary table of included users.
Select Exclude User.
Add additional users as needed.
Select Next.
Review Review the settings.
Use Previous to return to previous steps and make any changes if needed.
Select Apply to continue.

With this option, you will be scheduling to Deploy your Content Collection at a future date and time. After you select Later, the section Choose Date and Time to Deploy appear. This contains a calendar with the date and time as well as a few schedule shortcut options.
Schedule Later Deployments
You can select a future time to deploy by clicking one of the following shortcut buttons:
Deploy in 1 Hour
Deploy in 24 Hours
Deploy in 1 Week
Selecting an option above automatically advances the scheduled date and time to the corresponding choice. Custom Range - is the default option and allows you to select your own date and time. You can select any date in the future and any time in five-minute increments.
The time scheduled is in the time zone as in your Company in Master Settings.

Deployment Center
Contact Override Preference
When Creating a Deployment, once you have Selected Your Content Collection you will have the option to set to Contact Override Preference to Yes
On each Contact, you have a field to set Contact Preference with an option of different contact options:
Email
Home Phone
Mobile Phone
Text Messaging
When you send a Content Collection that contains both Email and Text Message by setting this to Yes Surefire will only send them the media type they prefer to receive in the Contact Preference.
If a Contact who tells you they prefer to be contacted by Email and you set their Contact Preference to Email. Later, when sending a Happy Holidays Content Collection that contains Email and Text Message, if you change the Contact Override Preference to Yes, they will only receive an Email and not an Text Message.
By default, your Deployment will ignore Contact Preference.

Marketing
Deployment Center
Build an Audience for a Deployment
Build an Audience for a Deployment Audiences by Media Type, based on the media you chose when you Selected a Content Collection, you will see different tabs to configure your Audiences. Click on a tab to Build Your Audience for that media. Overview - once you have selected Audiences for your Media, this tab will summarize the totals for each.
Social will always be an unknown total as you are simply posting to your Page or Pages. Email - select your Opt-Out List and Audience Target on this tab. Once your Target is chosen, you will see a table listing all of the valid Contacts that meet the requirements as well as the Email Audience Count in a green bubble.
From the table, you can: Search - Search any of the fields to find a specific Contact Exclude - Click the Exclude button on any row to Exclude that Contact from the Deployment Text Messaging - this tab is similar to Email except that there is no need for an Opt-Out List. Additionally, you must specify which Text Message Number you want to use for the Deployment.
If you have multiple Text Messaging Numbers associated with your account, select the Text Messaging Number using the list to choose the one you want.
If you don't have a Text Message number on your account, you cannot Deploy Text Message Media.
Review Acquire a Text Messaging Number for additional information. Social - Select which Social Account(s) you want to post to. You can select multiple if you have one or more setup with your Surefire Account.
Audience Target
For Email and Text Message Media, you must choose what subset of your Contacts you want to target for your Deployment:
All Valid Contacts
Contact Types
Contact Tags
Saved Group
You can only select one of these options and cannot combine multiple Audience Targets. Also, at any point, you can Reset Your Audience for a Media by clicking the button on its tab. Or, you can reset all media with the Reset Audience Builder button on the Overview tab.
Social does not have an Audience Target as you will be posting directly to your Page(s).
All Valid Contacts
This option is good if you just want to send out a communication to your entire database with no discrimination.
For Email, this targets any Contact with a valid email address that has not opted out. For Text Messaging, this targets all Contacts with a valid Mobile Phone who have not opted out.
Contact Types
If you want to get more specific, you can target Contact Types. For instance, you could target a Realtor Partner Contact Type if you have a news alert email about the housing industry you want them to read. When choosing Types, you have two options: Include - Type in the names of the Contact Types you want to receive the Deployment
Exclude
-If there are any Types you want to be sure to Exclude, add them here
Contact Tags
To narrow your audience even further, you can target Contact Tags. For instance, you could target Contacts with the Tag January Seminar that you applied to people who attended a seminar you recently held. Again, you have two options with this Audience: Include - Type in the names of the Tag or Tags you want to receive the Deployment Exclude - If there are any Tags you want to be sure to Exclude, add them here. This is helpful if you have a broad tag to include (e.g. Refi Candidate) but a message, such as promoting a new jumbo loan product, where you want to exclude a Tag (e.g. Bad Credit)
Saved Group
Your final choice is to target a previously Saved Group, either Dynamic or Static.
Should you have a very specific set of requirements for a group of Contacts that you would send to — such as Contact Type is Partner but Exclude those with Tag Competitor — it is recommended that you build a Group for this purpose. You will have much more control over your list this way.
If you choose a Dynamic Group, whatever Contacts are in that Group at the time of Deployment are who will receive your message. So if you send a weekly email newsletter to a Dynamic Group as a Recurring Deployment, the Group will update itself every week before it Deploys.
Recurring - For My Company
If you are creating a Recurring Deployment that is not For Myself but For My Company, you will NOT configure an Audience. This will be done on a User-by-User basis as they Subscribe.
Opt-Out List
For any Email Deployments, you must select an Opt-Out List before you Build an Audience. Should a Contact click the Unsubscribe link on an Email, they would then become part of whichever Opt-Out List was applied to the Deployment.
Exclusions
On the Exclusions tab, you can view a list of Contacts who are set to be Excluded from your Deployment.
Contact Preference
If you had previously set Use Contact's Media Preference to Yes, you will see that preference indicated next to the Contacts under the Show column, when you select an Email or Text Message Audience and any Contacts have been affected.
Any Contact who has both a valid Text Message and Email but has a Contact Preference set will only show up in the list of their preferred Media.

Exclude Contacts in Deployments
Sometimes when you are Building Your Audience for your Deployment, you may want to exclude a segment of your Contacts who you do not want to receive your Deployment.
You have a few options as to how you can Exclude Contacts from your Deployment:
Exclude Button
In the table of Contacts for Text Message and Email, you can select Exclude next to an individual Contact to remove them from that media type.
Tag Excludes
If targeting your Audience via Contact Tags, you can choose to Exclude Contacts of a particular Tag(s)
Review Exclusions
Once you have Built Your Audience, you can review which Contacts are Excluded by going to the Exclusions tab. Here there is table that will show you who has been Excluded as well as an Exclude Reason.
The Exclusions are divided into groups of: Email Exclusions - Contacts you manually Excluded or who have invalid Email Addresses Email Opt-Outs - Contacts who have unsubscribed from the Opt-Out List used in this Deployment Text Message Exclusions - Contacts you manually Excluded or who have previously identified invalid Mobile Phone numbers

Deployment Center
View Past Deployments
You can view the results of previous Deployments.
Go to Marketing, Deployment Center.
Select the Deployed tab.
This contains a summary of all Past Deployment details.
The table features similar data as the Scheduled tab along with a few additional data points: Successes - of the initial Audience Size the number of Contacts the Deployment successfully reached Failures - inversely, this is the number of Contacts who failed to receive your message. This can be due to bad email/phone or other email failures such as inbox full. SPAM Complaints - the number of recipients who marked your email as SPAM. If this number gets too high it can affect your Email Reputation
You can take the following actions: Deployment Types - Filter table by Deployment Type (One-Time, Recurring) and/or Media Type (Email, Text Messages, Social) Add/Remove Columns - Click Columns to add/remove any column other than Deployment Sort Columns - Click a Column header to sort in ascending or descending order Search - Type in the search box to find any Deployments by name
Select Deployment Name to bring up the Past Deployment Details.
In the Delivery at a Glance section you can review the following metrics regarding the delivery of your Deployment: Audience Count - Total Contacts sent to Emails or Text Messages Delivered - Total Emails or Text Messages delivered to the entire Audience Interactions - Clicks, Opens and Unsubscribe counts for emails
Warnings - Marked as Spam and Bounces for emails Dropped - in certain cases, we will drop a message to a specific email address in order to protect your sender reputation. We track bounces, spam reports, and unsubscribes for each of our users. If a user sends a message to an email address that exists on one of these lists (has already been marked as a bounce, spam or unsubscribed) we will automatically drop the message (i.e., not send to the address).
We do this so that we can protect your email reputation and keep messages reaching the inbox. Other reasons for drops include the email content triggered spam filters.
In the Deployment Configuration you can review the deployment details: Created by - User who created the Deployment Created on - Date/Time the Deployment was sent Collection - Content Collection delivered Media Type - Type of media from the Collection. Each Media Type will have its own separate Detail Deployment Type - One-Time or Recurring
Review the Audience section to see the contacts that were part of your audience.

Marketing
Deployment Center
Contact Opt Out Settings
There are two ways that a contact can opt out of email marketing:
Contact can click the Unsubscribe button on email
User can click Change Subscriptions on Contact and manage their settings
When a contact is opted out of email marketing, the following rules are obeyed:
Email Address Level
Opt outs occur on the email and not contact level. So if a contact (John Smith) for a user with email xyz@gmail.com opts out and there is another contact (Jane Smith) with the same xyz@gmail.com email address, both contacts will be opted out of emails.
Conversely, if either contact later changes their email address, they will no longer be opted out as the opt out was tied to the email address and not contact.
User Level Opts Outs
In large organizations, a contact that opts out will only have that opt out tied to the user’s opt out list who sent the email prompting the opt out. So if another user in that organization is working with a contact with that same email address, they will still be able to email them.
Contacts also have the option to opt out of individual user lists or to globally opt out of all of a user’s current and future opt-out lists, effectively completely opting out of all emails from that user.
Global Company Opt Outs
A contact can also choose to globally opt out of all current and future email lists for the entire organization. If a contact globally opts out, they will never receive any emails from anyone in that organization.

Deployment Center
Deploy your own Birthday or Holiday Content
You can create your own birthday and holiday deployment which provides a great way to stay in touch with prospects, past clients and referral partners. Depending on the occasion, you can choose among text messages, emails, social posts, and postcards. Digital options include personalized video greetings, animated GIF images, and static images. All greetings are branded.
It’s important to review and update pre-scheduled birthday and holiday greetings annually to ensure they still meet your goals, to prevent the deployment of content from prior years, and to check deployment dates for floating holidays, such as Thanksgiving, Memorial Day and Labor Day. If the Surefire team releases new content you like better later in the year, you can go in and update the content again.
Birthday greetings are typically scheduled through a birthday rule, and holiday greetings are typically scheduled through recurring deployments. You can: see what’s currently set up in your account in Deployment Center, Available Subscriptions. view details, such as frequency and audience, by clicking the name of the recurring deployment or rule. change the collection you’ll deploy or adjust the date for the new year, by clicking Edit Deployment in the top right corner. subscribe to any deployments you want to go from your account . The subscribe button is on the right next to each available subscription.

Select Birthday folder.
Alternatively, go to Public, Postcard Collections, Birthdays folder.
View Holiday Content

Open the Public folder, Digital Greetings.
